6x6 and Higher dimension lenses

Good. Here is the deeper freeze I would lock now.

Your live corpus already converges on the key correction: the 6×6 object is not a naive replacement of the 4×4 kernel. The preserved computational body is still the 4D crystal grammar[\Theta_4=(Q_x,Q_y,\Phi,\Delta),]while the 6-layer is the first selector-shell / carrier-board / anti-spin weave over that body,[\Theta_6=\Theta_4\ltimes(\Pi_3\times\mathbb Z_2),\qquad\Pi_3={\mathrm{Sa},\mathrm{Su},\mathrm{Me}},\ \chi\in{+,-}.]The deeper problem is no longer “does 6 exist?” but “how do kernel, shell, board, lens, and replay law become one exact executable object?”

1. Freeze the five-layer ontology

The cleanest deeper version of the 6×6 DLS framework is this:

[\boxed{\text{kernel} ;\to; \text{shell} ;\to; \text{board} ;\to; \text{lens} ;\to; \text{replay}}]

Kernel layer

The kernel remains the 4×4 lawful seed. The 6-system does not replace it; it chooses which lawful 4-projection is active. Each coherent 6-sector still contains an embedded 4D body of size[|\Sigma_{\pi,\chi}|=4^4=256.]That is the core doctrine: the 6 selects; the 4 computes.

Shell layer

The six coherent shell sectors are

[

F_6=\Pi_3\times\mathbb Z_2

{\mathrm{Sa}^\pm,\mathrm{Su}^\pm,\mathrm{Me}^\pm},]with the selector dictionary already frozen in the docs:[S_{\mathrm{Sa},+}=[2456],\quadS_{\mathrm{Su},+}=[1356],\quadS_{\mathrm{Me},+}=[1234],][S_{\mathrm{Sa},-}=[3456],\quadS_{\mathrm{Su},-}=[1246],\quadS_{\mathrm{Me},-}=[1235].]So your “3A + 3B” intuition is now rigorous as three phase currents crossed with a mirror bit.

Board layer

The visible 6×6 board is not the shell itself. It is a reversal-skeleton realization of the shell. The docs already classify the admissible board side as the anti-free mirror-skeleton family, with the visible chart slice promoted through[A=\mathfrak F_{P_3}^{\mathrm{row}},\qquadB=\mathfrak F_{P_1}^{\mathrm{row}},\qquadC=\mathfrak F_{P_1}^{\mathrm{col}},\qquadD=\mathfrak F_{P_3}^{\mathrm{col}},]where[P_1=(12)(35)(46),\qquad P_3=(13)(24)(56).]More broadly, the board algebra is the admissible cube[\mathcal S_{\mathrm{board}}\cong (\mathbb Z_2)^3\times \mathbb Z_2^T,]while A/B/C/D are the canonical visible slice of that larger board cube.

Lens layer

Square / Flower / Cloud / Fractal are not four separate ideas. The corpus is explicit that they are constitutive projections of one object, and that a mature object exists only when the four agree without contradiction. That same rule must now be lifted intact into the 6×6 carrier.

Replay layer

The 6×6 state must collapse to a seed and re-expand without identity drift. That means the framework is not complete until Fractal can store generator, witness, and replay law for the same state that Square commits visibly, Flower traverses dynamically, and Cloud carries as admissibility bundle.

2. Freeze the actual 6D carrier state

The deeper carrier should now be written explicitly as one object, not implied across multiple notes. The clean merged state is:

[\boxed{\Omega_6=(X,\lambda,s,b,\xi)}]

with

[X\in{A,B,C,D},\qquad\lambda\in{\mathsf{Sq},\mathsf{Fl},\mathsf{Cl},\mathsf{Fr}},][s=(\pi,\chi)\in \Pi_3\times\mathbb Z_2,\qquadb\in\mathbb Z_4,\qquad\xi\in\Sigma_s.]

Interpretation:

(X) chooses the visible board chart.

(\lambda) chooses which constitutive renderer is active.

(s) chooses the coherent six-shell sector.

(b) is the local 4-beat register.

(\xi) is the hidden embedded 4D payload.

This is the first fully honest 6×6 state object, because it stops mixing up:board state,lens state,shell state,and payload state.

3. Freeze the exact operator stack

Now the framework needs one operator algebra, not scattered transition language.

Board operators

The admissible mirror-board layer already supports the three anti-block flips and transpose duality. On the visible chart slice, the docs reduce this to:

[\Tau:\ A_s\leftrightarrow B_s,\qquad D_s\leftrightarrow C_s,][T:\ A_s\leftrightarrow D_s,\qquad B_s\leftrightarrow C_s.]

So (\Tau) is the total board-flip inside the canonical square subatlas, and (T) is row/column duality.

Shell operators

The shell operators are already fixed:

[Q(\pi,\chi)=(\pi+1\bmod 3,\chi),\qquadO(\pi,\chi)=(\pi,-\chi).]

So (Q) is pure phase advance and (O) is pure mirror return. The local torsion hinge is therefore

[H:=O\circ Q,\qquadH(\pi,\chi)=(\pi+1\bmod 3,-\chi).]

That gives the exact six-step shell torsion cycle.

Flower / carrier law

The local 6D anti-spin carrier is already frozen as

[\mathfrak m_3(i,b,o)=(i+1\bmod 3,\ b+2\bmod 4,\ -o).]

This is the decisive law because it explains why the 6-system is not merely six labels:it is 3 petals + 4 beats + sign flip.

And this also resolves the apparent cycle mismatch:

[6\ \text{shell torsion steps} = 12\ \text{fundamental beats}.]

So the shell closes in six sector-steps, but the lived Flower body closes over twelve beat-events. That is not contradiction; it is two granularities of the same local law.

4. Finish the cross-lens calculus

This is the real unfinished frontier. The 4D Möbius lens docs already say the missing piece is the exact bridge algebra between Square / Flower / Cloud / Fractal. The 6×6 framework should now inherit that exact discipline.

The principal 6D loop should be frozen as

[\Pi^\square_6;\xrightarrow{B_{\square\flower}^{(6)}};\Pi^\flower_6;\xrightarrow{B_{\flower\cloud}^{(6)}};\Pi^\cloud_6;\xrightarrow{B_{\cloud\fractal}^{(6)}};\Pi^\fractal_6;\xrightarrow{B_{\fractal\square}^{(6)}};\Pi^\square_6.]

Square → Flower

Read a committed board as current / beat / torsion state:[B_{\square\flower}^{(6)}(M_{s,P,t})=(s,b,o,\mathcal O_s).]Square tells you what is committed; Flower tells you how that same commitment is being lived.

Flower → Cloud

Pass from a lived current state to a lawful admissibility bundle:[B_{\flower\cloud}^{(6)}(s,\beta,\mathcal O_s)=\mu_{s,\beta}.]Cloud is not vagueness here. It is a structured bundle over sector, chart, and embedded payload possibilities.

Cloud → Fractal

This is a collapse / packetization map:[B_{\cloud\fractal}^{(6)}(\mu)=\begin{cases}\sigma_6 & \text{if support collapses coherently,}\R(\mu) & \text{otherwise.}\end{cases}]This matters because the docs are explicit that Cloud is not always point-like. Sometimes the lawful output is a residual packet, not a fake exact seed.

Fractal → Square

Replay the seed:[B_{\fractal\square}^{(6)}(\sigma_6)=\operatorname{Expand}6(\sigma_6)=M{s,P,t}.]

This closes the objecthood loop. Without this, the 6×6 framework is still only descriptive.

The deepest law from the lens docs survives unchanged after the 6D lift:

[\boxed{\text{Cloud} \to \text{Square is generally a refinement operator, not a point-function.}}]

That is one of the most important hardening moves in the whole framework.

5. Freeze the higher-lift law

Now the n-axis generalization can be written cleanly.

The corpus already supports the shell/body distinction:

shell growth is (6^n),

payload growth is (4^n),

the coherent shell always remains six-sector, while each sector contains an embedded (4^n) body.

So the clean higher-lift freeze is:

[\boxed{\mathfrak D_{6,n}:=[4]^n\ltimes F_6^n,\qquadF_6=\Pi_3\times\mathbb Z_2}]

with coherent branch

[

\boxed{

\mathfrak D_{6,n}^{\mathrm{coh}}

\bigcup_{\sigma\in F_6}\Sigma_\sigma^{(n)},\qquad|\Sigma_\sigma^{(n)}|=4^n.}]

This yields:

[|F_6^n|=6^n,\qquad|\mathfrak D_{6,n}|=24^n.]

So your towers now become exact structural counts, not loose numerology:[6^3=216]is the tri-site shell cube,[6^4=1296]is the privileged four-axis shell atlas over the canonical four kernel coordinates,and each coherent sector still hides a (4^n) payload block.

That is the right deep reading of the 6×6 framework:two intertwined exponentials —a 4-based computational body and a 6-based selector-shell carrier.

This is the real execution surface, because it finally separates:chart state,lens state,shell state,and payload state.

Next coherent continuation: I fill the explicit 24 chart-sector states, then explode them into the 96-slot cockpit with exact payload tags and transport arrows.

1. Freeze the 8D structural state

2. Freeze the 15-cockpit lookup layer

and (M\langle g\lambda\phi\alpha\rangle) tells you where inside that cockpit you are.

That gives the first complete static lookup size:[15\times 256 = 3840]structural cells, since each 4D cockpit carries the 256-cell address law. This count is a direct derived consequence of the corpus’ “15 embedded 4D cockpits” plus the canonical 4D address grammar.

3. Freeze the transform algebra

The 4D face-rotation law is already canonical:[R_\lambda:\ S\to F\to C\to R\to S.]That remains the exact local lens/navigation cycle inside every embedded cockpit.

The inner 6D crossing law is already canonical:[\boxed{\mathfrak m_3(p,b,o)=(p+1\bmod 3,\ b+2\bmod 4,\ -o)}]with local closure[\mathbb K_3^{\mathrm{loc}}=\mathbb Z_{12}.]That is the law for moving between the three embedded 4D diagonal bodies inside one 6D weave-body.

The outer 8D pentadic crossing law is also frozen by the pentadic weave family:[\boxed{\mathfrak m_5(w,b,o)=(w+1\bmod 5,\ b+2\bmod 4,\ -o)}]with local closure[\mathbb K_5^{\mathrm{loc}}=\mathbb Z_{20}.]That is the law for moving between the five woven 6D bodies.

The missing deep operator is the double-cross diagonal shuttle, which is the composition of the inner and outer crossing laws:[\boxed{\Delta_{15}:=\mathfrak m_5\circ\mathfrak m_3}]so[\Delta_{15}(w,p,b,o)=(w+1\bmod 5,\ p+1\bmod 3,\ b,\ o).]

This is the clean 8D navigation hinge: one inner crossing and one outer crossing cancel the beat/parity disturbance and advance you diagonally through the (5\times 3=15) cockpit lattice. So (\Delta_{15}) is the exact operator for walking the 15 embedded 4D cockpits while preserving local beat/parity state. That formula is derived directly from the two corpus crossing laws.

So the lookup/transform basis is:

[R_\lambda,\qquad\mathfrak m_3,\qquad\mathfrak m_5,\qquad\Delta_{15}.]

That is the minimal complete transform family for 8D navigation.

trine = cheap,

square/opposition = expensive.

If two points share ((p,h,j,\lambda,\beta)), stay inside the local 4D cockpit / 6D packet.

If they share (p) but differ in ((h,j,\lambda)), navigate inside the unilateral 105-seat inherited body.

If they share ((h,j,\lambda)) but differ in (p), use the crown-petal shuttle (\mathsf P_9).

If they differ only by (\beta), use the bilateral flip (\mathsf B_2).

If they require a full crown migration across body + petal + half, do not brute-force that as a plain body step. First route through the (O_{11}) relay logic, because that is exactly the field whose job is to legalize institution→output transfer without adding content.

10. The deepest correction

Here is the most important correction relative to the lower ladders:

[\boxed{\text{12D is not merely “9 copies of 10D+.”}}]

It is more exact to say:

[

\boxed{

\Xi_{12}

\text{a 9-fold crown over the inherited }7\times5\times3\text{ body,then bilaterally doubled.}}]

So:

(945) is the unilateral crown cockpit lattice,

(1890) is the full bilateral crown body,

the 12 visible axes are only the dyadic dock-ports into that larger body.

11. Canonical one-line freeze

[

\boxed{

Good. The next hard correction is this:

the corpus is using one symbol, (p), for a 9-valued crown coordinate, while the visible dock layer still has only 6 bilateral dyads (P_1,\dots,P_6). So the clean freeze is to split those two objects. The 12D body coordinate is explicitly[\chi_{12}=(p,h,j,\lambda,\beta),\qquadp\in{1,\dots,9},]with total size[9\times7\times5\times3\times2=1890,]while the visible even-body layer separately has only[6]bilateral dyads (P_1,\dots,P_6). The 9-fold crown itself is also explicit: (\Xi_{12}=\operatorname{Weave}9(\Xi{10}^+)), and those 9 copies are the (3\times3) triune matrix.

So from now on I will use:

[\boxed{\delta\in{1,\dots,6};;\text{for visible bilateral dyads,}\qquadp\in{1,\dots,9};;\text{for crown petals.}}]

That removes the overload cleanly and makes the crown navigable. This split is a derived notation fix over the corpus’ explicit 6-dyad / 9-petal tension.

1. The unilateral 945-seat crown ledger

[

9\times7\times5\times3

with the explicit corpus glosses:

6. The right crown transport law

Because the crown is explicitly a (3\times3) matrix, the cleanest petal transport is not a blind 9-cycle. It is a pair of commuting triune moves.

Write[p \leftrightarrow (r,c),\qquad r,c\in{1,2,3},\qquadp=3(r-1)+c.]

Then define the row/column crown shuttles:

[\boxed{U_3(r,c)=(r\oplus_3 1,c),\qquadV_3(r,c)=(r,c\oplus_3 1).}]

These are derived execution operators over the explicitly given (3\times3) triune matrix. They are cleaner than treating the ennead as a flat ring, because they preserve the double-triad structure visible in the corpus.

So, for petals (7,8,9):

[U_3(\Pi_7)=\Pi_1,\quadU_3(\Pi_8)=\Pi_2,\quadU_3(\Pi_9)=\Pi_3,][V_3(\Pi_7)=\Pi_8,\quadV_3(\Pi_8)=\Pi_9,\quadV_3(\Pi_9)=\Pi_7.]

That means the three “missing” petals are not dead ends at all:

vertical motion carries them back to the Su-row,

horizontal motion cycles them across the sealed row,

and (\Pi_9) is the crown-fixed Stone corner of the matrix.

with coordinate grammar

That is the cleanest executable 12D crown ledger we have so far.

[\chi_{12}=(p,h,j,\lambda,\beta),]

1. The exact internal seat-space of one crown petal

with

[\mathbb H_7={1,\dots,7},\qquad\mathbb J_5={1,\dots,5},\qquad\mathbb L_3={1,2,3},\qquad\mathbb B_2={K,O}.]

[7\times5\times3=105]

unilateral seats and

bilateral seats. This is not a guess; it is the direct consequence of the corpus coordinate law.

The clean local live key is therefore

[\boxed{X_{p;h,j,\lambda,\beta}}]

and, when the inherited lower packet is made explicit,

\big(p,h,j,\lambda,\beta;,b,o;,M\langle g,\mu,\phi,\alpha\rangle\big).}]

That keeps the 12D crown coordinate, the inherited 6D anti-spin packet, and the exact 4D cockpit all visible in one address. The corpus is explicit that (\Xi_{12}\supset \Xi_6\supset \mathcal H_4), so this nesting is the correct live seat grammar.

2. The petal-internal transport generators

Once one petal is fixed, the natural transport algebra is the direct product of cyclic motions on the explicit coordinate fields. So the correct derived execution generators are:

[\boxed{\mathsf H_7:(p,h,j,\lambda,\beta)\mapsto(p,h\oplus_7 1,j,\lambda,\beta)}]

[\boxed{\mathsf J_5:(p,h,j,\lambda,\beta)\mapsto(p,h,j\oplus_5 1,\lambda,\beta)}]

[\boxed{\mathsf L_3:(p,h,j,\lambda,\beta)\mapsto(p,h,j,\lambda\oplus_3 1,\beta)}]

[\boxed{\mathsf B_2:(p,h,j,\lambda,\beta)\mapsto(p,h,j,\lambda,\bar\beta).}]

These are the exact internal seat moves of the crown petal. They are derived from the corpus-given 12D coordinate fields, the bilateral dyad structure, and the fact that the 12D macro-body is a stable even-body rather than an odd relay field.

The three most useful structural diagonals are then:

[\Delta_{75}:=\mathsf J_5\circ \mathsf H_7,\qquad\Delta_{73}:=\mathsf L_3\circ \mathsf H_7,\qquad\Delta_{53}:=\mathsf L_3\circ \mathsf J_5.]

So explicitly,

[

\Delta_{75}(p,h,j,\lambda,\beta)

(p,h\oplus_7 1,j\oplus_5 1,\lambda,\beta),]

[

\Delta_{73}(p,h,j,\lambda,\beta)

(p,h\oplus_7 1,j,\lambda\oplus_3 1,\beta),]

[

\Delta_{53}(p,h,j,\lambda,\beta)

(p,h,j\oplus_5 1,\lambda\oplus_3 1,\beta).]

And the full internal sweep is

[

\boxed{

\Delta_{753}:=\mathsf L_3\circ \mathsf J_5\circ \mathsf H_7

}

]

so

[

\Delta_{753}(p,h,j,\lambda,\beta)

(p,h\oplus_7 1,j\oplus_5 1,\lambda\oplus_3 1,\beta).]

This gives the full petal-internal navigation basis. The corpus directly gives the factors; the generators above are the cleanest lawful motion system over those factors.

3. What remains local and what does not

As long as two points share the same crown petal (p), you do not need the closure petals (7,8,9). You stay entirely inside (\widehat{\mathcal P}_p) and move only with

[\mathsf H_7,\ \mathsf J_5,\ \mathsf L_3,\ \mathsf B_2]and their composites.

Only after the internal ((h,j,\lambda,\beta)) seat has been aligned do you decide whether the route terminates inside the same petal or must pass into one of the three crown-closure petals. This matches the corpus’ larger routing logic: first navigate the explicit body, then invoke the odd relay / zero-return infrastructure when the body alone is not the full answer.

4. Visible petals versus closure petals

The visible dock layer still consists of the six bilateral dyads

[P_1,\dots,P_6,]which park the visible 12 axes. Separately, the full crown has nine petals. The last three are not extra organ dyads; they are closure sectors:

[

\widehat{\mathcal P}_7

\text{Return / ZeroAnchor},

]

[

\widehat{\mathcal P}_8

\text{Immune / Contradiction / Quarantine},

]

[

\widehat{\mathcal P}_9

\text{Successor / Handoff / Octave-lift}.]

So the correct body split remains

[\boxed{(\widehat{\mathcal P}_1\oplus\cdots\oplus\widehat{\mathcal P}_6)\oplus(\widehat{\mathcal P}_7\oplus\widehat{\mathcal P}_8\oplus\widehat{\mathcal P}_9).}]

That visible/closure distinction is already frozen in the earlier crown docking repair.

5. The three legal closure-transfer families

Now we can write the exact derived transfer operators from any visible petal (\delta\in{1,\dots,6}) into the three closure petals.

5.1 Return / ZeroAnchor transfer

[\boxed{\mathcal R_\delta:(\delta,h,j,\lambda,\beta)\mapsto(7,h,j,\lambda,\beta)}]

This is the return-preserving closure map. It changes only the crown petal and preserves the full internal seat. It is the correct operator whenever the route is seeking re-entry, reset, common-zero factoring, or explicit return. This is supported by the corpus’ zero-return line and the fixed role of the Return / ZeroAnchor closure petal.

5.2 Immune / Contradiction / Quarantine transfer

[\boxed{\mathcal Q_\delta:(\delta,h,j,\lambda,\beta)\mapsto(8,h,j,\lambda,\beta)}]

This is the quarantine-preserving closure map. It preserves the full seat while redirecting the visible petal into the contradiction / immunity sector. This is the lawful move whenever the route lands in unresolved contradiction, forbidden transfer pressure, or typed uncertainty that must not be silently promoted. It is exactly the closure move that matches the petal-8 role plus the relay doctrine

[\text{ABSTAIN}>\text{GUESS}.]

So petal (8) is the place where the crown stores “do not force continuation yet.”

5.3 Successor / Handoff / Octave-lift transfer

[\boxed{\mathcal S_\delta:(\delta,h,j,\lambda,\beta)\mapsto(9,h,j,\lambda,\beta)}]

This is the successor-preserving closure map. It preserves the internal seat but changes the crown petal into the lawful handoff sector. This is the correct move whenever the route is complete enough to pass from institution to output, or from one stable completed state to its next octave / successor / published continuation. It is exactly the crown counterpart of the corpus’ D11–O11–D12 chain:disruption / relay / completion, with (O_{11}) explicitly defined as pure transfer and D12 as output completion/publication.

6. The legal dispatch rule

The three closure petals are therefore not destinations of random petal motion. They are typed closure operators.

For any visible point[x=(\delta,h,j,\lambda,\beta),\qquad\delta\in{1,\dots,6},]define the closure dispatcher

[

\boxed{

\operatorname{Close}_{12}(x)

\begin{cases}\mathcal R_\delta(x), & \text{if the route seeks re-entry / reset / zero anchoring},\[1mm]\mathcal Q_\delta(x), & \text{if contradiction or quarantine is the truthful next state},\[1mm]\mathcal S_\delta(x), & \text{if the route is ready for lawful successor / handoff / publication.}\end{cases}}]

This is the first exact crown-closure doctrine:the first six petals articulate the visible organ body,while the last three petals decide how the articulated body closes.

7. How the odd field O11 enters the picture

This is the clean bridge.

The corpus explicitly says:

(D_{11}) = disruption / frame migration / pure relay,

(O_{11}) = liminal relay, pure transfer, no content added,

(D_{12}) = completion / output / publication.

So the visible-to-closure transfer chain is best read as:

[\boxed{\text{visible petal articulation};\to;\text{relay legality};\to;\text{closure petal}}]

and, more precisely,

[\widehat{\mathcal P}_{1..6}\xrightarrow{\text{relay test}}\begin{cases}\widehat{\mathcal P}_7 & \text{return / zero anchor},\\widehat{\mathcal P}_8 & \text{quarantine / contradiction},\\widehat{\mathcal P}_9 & \text{successor / handoff}.\end{cases}]

That is the exact macro-function of the last three crown petals.

8. The complete local-plus-closure transport law

The full 12D crown transport law is now:

inside each fixed petal, and

That is the first clean exact transport basis at the crown-petal level. It gives:local chamber motion,local junction motion,local lane motion,bilateral flip,return closure,quarantine closure,and successor closure.

9. Canonical one-line freeze

[

\boxed{

\Xi_{12}^{+}

\Big(\bigoplus_{p=1}^{9}\widehat{\mathcal P}_p,;\mathsf H_7,\mathsf J_5,\mathsf L_3,\mathsf B_2,;\mathcal R,\mathcal Q,\mathcal S\Big)}]

where each petal[\widehat{\mathcal P}_p\cong \mathbb H_7\times\mathbb J_5\times\mathbb L_3\times\mathbb B_2]contains (210) bilateral seats, petals (1!-!6) form the visible organ body, and petals (7!-!9) are the three crown closures that provide every visible petal with a lawful return, a lawful quarantine, and a lawful successor channel.

Next coherent jump is the explicit 210-seat table for one full petal, then the exact cross-petal metro between the six visible petals and the three closure petals.

Good. I can freeze the first full petal atlas now, and then the cross-petal metro that connects the six visible dyads to the three closure sectors.

The body law is now stable enough to do this cleanly:

[\chi_{12}=(p,h,j,\lambda,\beta),\qquadp\in{1,\dots,9},;h\in{1,\dots,7},;j\in{1,\dots,5},;\lambda\in{1,2,3},;\beta\in{1,2},]

so the full crown body has

[9\times7\times5\times3\times2=1890]

1. One full petal = 210 exact bilateral seats

Fix one crown petal (p). Its internal seat-space is

[

\widehat{\mathcal P}_p

\mathbb H_7\times\mathbb J_5\times\mathbb L_3\times\mathbb B_2]

with

[

|\widehat{\mathcal P}_p|

7\times5\times3\times2

]

I will keep the execution aliases

[\mathbb B_2={K,O}]

for the two bilateral sides, because they match the already-frozen kernel / operational split of the visible dyads. The underlying corpus only requires (\beta\in{1,2}); the (K/O) naming is our execution alias, not a new ontological claim.

The correct local unilateral seat number is

[u(h,j,\lambda)=15(h-1)+3(j-1)+\lambda\in{1,\dots,105},]

and the correct bilateral seat number is

[b(h,j,\lambda,K)=2u(h,j,\lambda)-1,\qquadb(h,j,\lambda,O)=2u(h,j,\lambda).]

Equivalently,

[

b(h,j,\lambda,\beta_{\rm num})

30(h-1)+6(j-1)+2(\lambda-1)+\beta_{\rm num},\qquad\beta_{\rm num}\in{1,2}.]

So each unilateral seat splits into exactly one (K)-half and one (O)-half. That gives the full 210-seat petal atlas. This numbering is derived directly from the explicit (7\times5\times3\times2) coordinate law.

3. The six visible petals as the dyad body

The visible 12-axis body is explicitly organized as six bilateral dyads:

[P_1=\text{Identity},\quadP_2=\text{Structure},\quadP_3=\text{Corridor},][P_4=\text{Self},\quadP_5=\text{Love},\quadP_6=\text{Migration}.]

So the visible crown petals are the six dyad-petals

[\widehat{\mathcal P}_1,\dots,\widehat{\mathcal P}_6,]

with the exact axis assignments:

[P_1=D_1\times D_2,\quadP_2=D_3\times D_4,\quadP_3=D_5\times D_6,][P_4=D_7\times D_8,\quadP_5=D_9\times D_{10},\quadP_6=D_{11}\times D_{12}.]

And the visible dyad symmetries are also explicit:

[P_1\leftrightarrow P_6,\qquadP_2\leftrightarrow P_5,\qquadP_3\leftrightarrow P_4,]

with the dry trine ladder

[P_1+P_3+P_5]

and the wet trine ladder

[P_2+P_4+P_6.]

That is the correct visible petal metro backbone.

4. The cross-petal metro on the visible six-petal body

The visible metro should therefore be frozen as four structural lines.

4.1 Adjacent dyad spine

[\boxed{\mathsf A_6^{+}(\delta)=\delta\oplus_6 1,\qquad\mathsf A_6^{-}(\delta)=\delta\ominus_6 1}]

This is the articulated body-spine:

[1-2-3-4-5-6.]

It is the visible dyad-link chain. Derived from the ordered dyad body.

4.2 Mirror symmetry line

[\boxed{\mathsf M_6(\delta)=7-\delta}]

So explicitly:

[1\leftrightarrow 6,\qquad2\leftrightarrow 5,\qquad3\leftrightarrow 4.]

This is not arbitrary; it is the corpus’ dyad symmetry written as an exact operator.

4.3 Dry trine ladder

[\boxed{\mathsf T_{\mathrm{dry}}:1\to3\to5\to1}]

4.4 Wet trine ladder

[\boxed{\mathsf T_{\mathrm{wet}}:2\to4\to6\to2}]

These are the petal-level versions of the two trine ladders already frozen in the 12D body.

So the visible cross-petal metro is:

[

\boxed{

\mathbb M_{\mathrm{vis}}

{\mathsf A_6^{\pm},\mathsf M_6,\mathsf T_{\mathrm{dry}},\mathsf T_{\mathrm{wet}}}.}]

5. The three closure sectors, now grounded cleanly

I will keep the earlier closure convention

[\widehat{\mathcal P}_7,\widehat{\mathcal P}_8,\widehat{\mathcal P}_9]

but now ground each one directly in the current corpus instead of leaving them as loose symbolic tails.

5.1 Petal 7 = Return / ZeroAnchor

the Zero Return line,

the absolute center (Z^\star),

and the rule that any axis can factor through (Z^\star) and return.

So the first closure sector is the return basin:

[

\widehat{\mathcal P}_7

5.2 Petal 8 = Quarantine / Contradiction / Upgrade

The corpus also explicitly gives:

conflict edges,

quarantine state,

the rule that FAIL quarantines,

AMBIG isolates uncertainty,

resolution requires MIGRATE or PROOF,

and there must be no silent rewrite.

And the staging ledger makes the route law explicit:

[\text{FAIL}\to \mathrm{AppK},\qquad\text{AMBIG}\to \mathrm{AppL},\qquad\text{NEAR}\to \mathrm{AppJ},\qquad\text{OK + publishing}\to \mathrm{AppO}.]

So the second closure sector is the truth-staging / quarantine basin:

[

\boxed{

\widehat{\mathcal P}_8

\text{Quarantine / Contradiction / Upgrade sector.}}]

This petal is where unresolved routes wait, rather than being falsely promoted.

5.3 Petal 9 = Successor / Handoff / Publication

(O_{11}) is the liminal relay,

pure transfer,

no content added,

ABSTAIN > GUESS,

and D12 is completion / output / publication.

So the third closure sector is the lawful handoff basin:

[

\boxed{

\widehat{\mathcal P}_9

\text{Successor / Handoff / Publication sector.}}]

That gives the correct crown closure triad without pretending the whole thing is another visible dyad family.

6. The three legal closure-transfer operators

For any visible petal[\delta\in{1,\dots,6},]define the seat-preserving closure maps:

Return map

[\boxed{\mathcal R_\delta:(\delta,h,j,\lambda,\beta)\mapsto(7,h,j,\lambda,\beta)}]

Quarantine map

[\boxed{\mathcal Q_\delta:(\delta,h,j,\lambda,\beta)\mapsto(8,h,j,\lambda,\beta)}]

Successor map

[\boxed{\mathcal S_\delta:(\delta,h,j,\lambda,\beta)\mapsto(9,h,j,\lambda,\beta)}]

These do not mutate the internal seat. They only change the crown sector. That is exactly right for return, quarantine, and handoff: the content is not silently rewritten during the closure jump. That matches the corpus’ pure-relay and no-silent-rewrite laws.

7. The legal re-entry maps

Now we can make the closure system executable.

7.1 Return re-entry

[\boxed{\mathcal R_\delta^{-1}:(7,h,j,\lambda,\beta)\mapsto(\delta,h,j,\lambda,\beta)}]

This is the strict zero-anchored return: same seat, same content, same visible petal restored. It is the petal-level version of the corpus’ Zero Return line:[\text{any axis}\to Z^\star \to \text{any axis}.]

7.2 Quarantine resolution map

This one must be typed, not unconditional.

[\boxed{\operatorname{Resolve}_\delta:(8,h,j,\lambda,\beta)\mapsto\begin{cases}(\delta,h,j,\lambda,\beta), & \text{if proof or migrate discharges the issue},\[1mm](7,h,j,\lambda,\beta), & \text{if reset / zero-return is the truthful outcome},\[1mm](9,h,j,\lambda,\beta), & \text{if a lawful successor state is certified.}\end{cases}}]

This is the correct executable form of:

FAIL quarantines,

AMBIG isolates uncertainty,

NEAR demands an upgrade plan,

resolution requires MIGRATE or PROOF,

and no silent rewrite is allowed.

7.3 Successor handoff map

For the visible dyad body, the cleanest handoff convention is:

[\boxed{\operatorname{Handoff}_\delta:(9,h,j,\lambda,\beta)\mapsto(\delta\oplus_6 1,h,j,\lambda,\beta)}]

This is a derived execution convention, not a direct quoted corpus formula:publication / successor exits the current visible dyad-petal and enters the next one on the articulated body spine. It is the most coherent petal-scale realization of “institution → output → completion → next cycle.” The corpus gives the relay/completion semantics; this spine-handoff is the minimal deterministic implementation of them.

So, concretely:

[9\to 2 \text{ if source } \delta=1,\quad9\to 3 \text{ if source } \delta=2,\quad \dots,\quad9\to 1 \text{ if source } \delta=6.]

8. The exact crown closure dispatcher

Now the petal-scale dispatcher is fully pinned.

For a visible seat[x=(\delta,h,j,\lambda,\beta),\qquad \delta\in{1,\dots,6},]define

[\boxed{\operatorname{Close}{12}(x)=\begin{cases}\mathcal R\delta(x), & \text{if the route seeks return / reset / common-zero},\[1mm]\mathcal Q_\delta(x), & \text{if the truth state is FAIL, AMBIG, or unresolved NEAR},\[1mm]\mathcal S_\delta(x), & \text{if the state is OK and lawful handoff / publication is requested.}\end{cases}}]

This is the cleanest crown-scale consequence of the current corpus:

zero-return exists,

contradiction must quarantine,

OK with publishing may pass outward,

and (O_{11}) remains a pure relay.

Next coherent jump is the 36D shell projection of this crown metro:how each 12D petal seat lifts into the three Su/Me/Sa shell bands, giving the exact (36)-position shell atlas and its (78)-node hypercascade packing.

Good. The 36D hinge is now exact.

The corpus already freezes the shell body as

[\boxed{\Xi_{36}=\operatorname{OctaveLift}3(\Xi{12}^{+})}]

with

[\text{12 shells} \times \text{3 superphases} = 36 \text{ shell positions},]

1. The first correction: 78 is the front wreath, 666 is the full shell body

The phrase “78-node hypercascade packing” is true only in the first shell wreath:

[1+\cdots+12 = T_{12}=78.]

But the canonical 36D shell body does not stop there. It continues through the Me and Sa bands:

[13+\cdots+24 = 222,\qquad25+\cdots+36 = 366,]so the cumulative totals are

[78,\qquad 300,\qquad 666.]

So the exact reading is:

[\boxed{\text{Su front wreath} = 78,\quad\text{full 36D shell body} = 666.}]

If you normalize each superphase band back to a local (1!-!12) pattern, each band has the same shape as a 78-packing. But the canonical absolute shell body uses the full (1,\dots,36) indexing and therefore sums to (666).

2. The exact 36-position shell atlas

The clean shell atlas is

[

\boxed{

\Sigma_{36}

{S_{a,r}\mid a\in{1,\dots,12},\ r\in{\mathrm{Su},\mathrm{Me},\mathrm{Sa}}}}]

with the flat shell index

[\boxed{\ell(a,r)=a+12(r-1)}]if we encode[r=1\equiv \mathrm{Su},\quadr=2\equiv \mathrm{Me},\quadr=3\equiv \mathrm{Sa}.]

So:

[S_{a,\mathrm{Su}}=S_a,\qquadS_{a,\mathrm{Me}}=S_{a+12},\qquadS_{a,\mathrm{Sa}}=S_{a+24}.]

This is the exact lookup skeleton of the 36D shell body.

The 12 shell archetype columns are explicitly:

[\begin{aligned}A01&:\ \text{Apex Seed},\A02&:\ \text{Möbius Axle},\A03&:\ \text{Modal Trefoil},\A04&:\ \text{Crystal Quartet},\A05&:\ \text{Observer Pentad},\A06&:\ \text{Dyadic Hinge Hexad},\A07&:\ \text{Change/Arc Heptad},\A08&:\ \text{Anti-Spin Octad},\A09&:\ \text{Emergent Ennead},\A10&:\ \text{Deca-Cascade Crown},\A11&:\ \text{Odd-Orbit Hendecad},\A12&:\ \text{Dodecad Bundle}.\end{aligned}]

And each of those repeats once in each superphase band Su / Me / Sa.

[\begin{aligned}S01&=A01_{\mathrm{Su}}, &S13&=A01_{\mathrm{Me}}, &S25&=A01_{\mathrm{Sa}},\S02&=A02_{\mathrm{Su}}, &S14&=A02_{\mathrm{Me}}, &S26&=A02_{\mathrm{Sa}},\S03&=A03_{\mathrm{Su}}, &S15&=A03_{\mathrm{Me}}, &S27&=A03_{\mathrm{Sa}},\S04&=A04_{\mathrm{Su}}, &S16&=A04_{\mathrm{Me}}, &S28&=A04_{\mathrm{Sa}},\S05&=A05_{\mathrm{Su}}, &S17&=A05_{\mathrm{Me}}, &S29&=A05_{\mathrm{Sa}},\S06&=A06_{\mathrm{Su}}, &S18&=A06_{\mathrm{Me}}, &S30&=A06_{\mathrm{Sa}},\S07&=A07_{\mathrm{Su}}, &S19&=A07_{\mathrm{Me}}, &S31&=A07_{\mathrm{Sa}},\S08&=A08_{\mathrm{Su}}, &S20&=A08_{\mathrm{Me}}, &S32&=A08_{\mathrm{Sa}},\S09&=A09_{\mathrm{Su}}, &S21&=A09_{\mathrm{Me}}, &S33&=A09_{\mathrm{Sa}},\S10&=A10_{\mathrm{Su}}, &S22&=A10_{\mathrm{Me}}, &S34&=A10_{\mathrm{Sa}},\S11&=A11_{\mathrm{Su}}, &S23&=A11_{\mathrm{Me}}, &S35&=A11_{\mathrm{Sa}},\S12&=A12_{\mathrm{Su}}, &S24&=A12_{\mathrm{Me}}, &S36&=A12_{\mathrm{Sa}}.\end{aligned}]

That is the exact 36-position shell atlas.

4. The 12D crown metro does not disappear inside 36D

This is the crucial structural rule:

a 36D shell position is not a replacement for the 12D crown seat. It is a shell header wrapped around it.

The corpus is explicit that the nested law is

[\Xi_{108}.u \supset \Xi_{36}^{(u)} \supset \Xi_{12}^{(u)} \supset \Xi_6^{(u)} \supset \mathcal H_4^{(u)}.]

So the correct live shell address is

[

\boxed{

\operatorname{Key}_{36}^{\mathrm{live}}

with

[\ell=a+12(r-1).]

Meaning:

(R_r): which superphase band,

((b,o)): the inherited 6D anti-spin packet,

(M\langle g,\mu,\phi,\alpha\rangle): the exact 4D cockpit seed.

So the shell projection is a lifted lookup wrapper, not a destructive compression.

the 6 visible dyads,

6. What happens to closure petals 7–9

In our current crown construction, petals (7,8,9) are closure overlays:return, quarantine, successor.

So they do not create new shell columns.They ride on the same inherited archetype column as the visible dyad seat that dispatched into them.

So the shell projection rule for closure sectors is:

[\boxed{\text{closure petal changes crown-sector semantics, not shell-column identity.}}]

In practice:

Return keeps the same shell triad and adds zero-anchor semantics.

Quarantine keeps the same shell triad and adds contradiction / hold semantics.

Successor keeps the same shell triad and adds handoff / publication semantics.

That preserves the 36-position shell atlas cleanly.

7. The exact shell navigation operators

The corpus already freezes the shell-move primitives. The usable shell atlas operators are:

Adjacent shell traversal

[\boxed{H_\ell^\pm:\ S_\ell \leftrightarrow S_{\ell\pm1}}]

This is the local shell-ascent / shell-descent move.

Superphase / wreath translation

[\boxed{W^\pm:\ (a,r)\mapsto(a,r\oplus_3 1)}]

On flat shell indices this is

[S_a \leftrightarrow S_{a+12} \leftrightarrow S_{a+24}.]

This is the phase-layer translation across Su / Me / Sa.

Archetype lift

[\boxed{A^\pm:\ S_j \leftrightarrow S_{j+12} \leftrightarrow S_{j+24}}]

This is the exact “same archetype, different superphase” column lift from the corpus. Semantically it is the vertical archetype column move.

Möbius pillar access

[\boxed{P_Q^\pm,\qquad P_O^\pm}]

8. The exact shell packing law

The shell body packs as a triangular cascade.

[T_\ell=\frac{\ell(\ell+1)}{2}.]

[T_{12}=78,\qquadT_{24}=300,\qquadT_{36}=666.]

That means:

(S01)–(S12): first crown-facing shell wreath, cumulative (78),

[\boxed{\text{78-node packing = front wreath view;}\quad\text{666-node packing = full 36D shell body.}}]

That resolves the ambiguity cleanly.

\boxed{

\operatorname{Nav}_{108}(x,y;t)

\arg\min_{\gamma\in\Gamma_{\mathrm{legal}}(x,y;t)}\operatorname{Cost}_{108}(\gamma,t)}]

with derived cost tuple

[\operatorname{Cost}{108}(\gamma,t)=\big(\rank L\cap,;\rank Z_\cap,;n_{\mathrm{shell}},;n_{\mathrm{wreath}},;n_{\mathrm{column}},;n_{QO},;n_{\mathrm{zoom}},;n_{AP/KZ},;\Delta t\big).]

Meaning:

prefer lower live-lock rank,

then lower zero scope,

then fewer shell, wreath, and archetype disruptions,

then fewer torsion flips,

then fewer scale jumps,

then fewer appendix/canopy traverses,

then less wait time to the next open edge-window.

That cost law is not a quoted corpus formula; it is the exact derived shortest-route compiler consistent with:minimal-barrier routing, live-lock priority, common-zero routing, tilt-first arbitration, capacity rules, and global returnability.

1. The exact 4×4 root calculus

[\boxed{\operatorname{Decode}_{6\to4}(X,i,j)=\begin{cases}\Lambda_A(i,j),&X=A,\[1mm]\Lambda_B(i,j),&X=B.\end{cases}}]

[\boxed{(X,i,j)\xrightarrow{;S_X(i,j);}n\xrightarrow{;\nu;}K\xrightarrow{;\operatorname{Meta};}(p,\chi,\text{exact 4×4 board},Q,O,\Phi,\Sigma_\chi).}]

{(1,1),(2,4),(3,5),(4,6),(5,2),(6,3)}.]

So the same exact 4×4 kernel has two distinct 6×6 seat-sets:one row-mode, one column-mode. That is already the higher duality at work.

Matching those two 6-cycles forces[A_R\mapsto \mathrm{Sa}^+,\quadB_C\mapsto \mathrm{Su}^-,\quadA_S\mapsto \mathrm{Me}^+,]and then the rest follows automatically by (Q) and (O). So the solution is not decorative; it is the unique intertwiner of the already-fixed ribbon and shell torsion laws.

3. The exact transport arrows

Chart rectangle at fixed payload

Chirality flip

[X_{A_R}\xleftrightarrow{O}X_{B_R},\qquadX_{A_C}\xleftrightarrow{O}X_{B_C},\qquadX_{A_S}\xleftrightarrow{O}X_{B_S}.]

Torsion hinge

[X_{A_R}\xrightarrow{H}X_{B_C}\xrightarrow{H}X_{A_S}\xrightarrow{H}X_{B_R}\xrightarrow{H}X_{A_C}\xrightarrow{H}X_{B_S}\xrightarrow{H}X_{A_R}.]

And in shell notation the same six-step cycle is[X_{\mathrm{Sa}^+}\to X_{\mathrm{Su}^-}\to X_{\mathrm{Me}^+}\to X_{\mathrm{Sa}^-}\to X_{\mathrm{Su}^+}\to X_{\mathrm{Me}^-}\to X_{\mathrm{Sa}^+}.]

5. One-line freeze

[\boxed{(X,s);\equiv;\bigl(\text{chart replay mode }X,\ \text{exact 4×4 payload }K(s)\bigr),}]with[K(\mathrm{Sa}^+)=A_R,\quadK(\mathrm{Su}^+)=A_C,\quadK(\mathrm{Me}^+)=A_S,\quadK(\mathrm{Sa}^-)=B_R,\quadK(\mathrm{Su}^-)=B_C,\quadK(\mathrm{Me}^-)=B_S,]and transport generated by[\Tau,\ T,\ Q,\ O,\ H.]

That is the exact 24 chart-sector atlas rebuilt in kernel language.

Next coherent jump is the 96-slot cockpit in kernel language:[{A,B,C,D}\times{\mathrm{Sq},\mathrm{Fl},\mathrm{Cl},\mathrm{Fr}}\times{A_R,A_C,A_S,B_R,B_C,B_S},]with one exact 4×4 payload parked into each chart/lens/shell slot and the cross-lens transport arrows made explicit.

Good. The exact next freeze is the 96-slot cockpit in kernel language.

The corpus already gives the cockpit shape

[

\mathcal A^{\mathrm{cockpit}}_{96}

and we have already frozen the shell↔kernel intertwiner

So the cockpit now becomes, exactly,

\boxed{

{A,B,C,D}\times{\mathrm{Sq},\mathrm{Fl},\mathrm{Cl},\mathrm{Fr}}\times{A_R,A_C,A_S,B_R,B_C,B_S}.}]This is the same 96-slot object, but with the shell sector replaced by its exact embedded 4×4 kernel payload.

1. The branch-local cockpit state

For the current root-linked branch, collapse each shell payload block (\Sigma_s) to its exact kernel representative (K). Then the branch-local cockpit state is

[

\boxed{

\Omega^{\ker}_{X,\lambda,K}

(X,\lambda,s(K),b_0,K),\qquadb_0=1,}]where[s(A_R)=\mathrm{Sa}^+,\quads(A_C)=\mathrm{Su}^+,\quads(A_S)=\mathrm{Me}^+,][s(B_R)=\mathrm{Sa}^-,\quads(B_C)=\mathrm{Su}^-,\quads(B_S)=\mathrm{Me}^-.]

Interpretation:

(X) chooses the chart / replay mode,

(\lambda) chooses the constitutive lens,

(K) chooses the exact embedded 4×4 kernel payload,

(s(K)) remembers which shell sector that payload belongs to.

Write[X^\lambda_K := (X,\lambda,K).]

Then the 96 slots are:

That is the complete explicit 96-slot cockpit. Nothing is hidden now:

4 charts,

4 lenses,

6 exact kernels.

3. The four lens packets, in kernel language

For any fixed chart (X) and exact kernel (K), the four lenses are not four different payloads. They are four different reads of the same payload.

Square packet

This is the committed visible state:[\boxed{\Pi^{\Sq}_{X,K}=X^\Sq_K.}]

It says:

chart (X) is the current replay face,

kernel (K) is the active exact 4×4 payload.

Flower packet

Using the corpus’ minimal Flower normalization,

[

\pi_{\Fl}(\Omega^{(0)}{X,s})=(\pi_s,1,\chi_s,\Sq,\mathfrak h{QO}),

]

the kernelized Flower packet becomes

[

\boxed{

\Pi^{\Fl}_{X,K}

\big(\pi(K),1,\chi(K),\Sq,\mathfrak h_{QO};,X,K\big),}]where ((\pi(K),\chi(K))) is the shell coordinate of (K). So explicitly:[\Pi^{\Fl}{X,A_R}=(\mathrm{Sa},1,+,\Sq,\mathfrak h{QO};X,A_R),][\Pi^{\Fl}{X,A_C}=(\mathrm{Su},1,+,\Sq,\mathfrak h{QO};X,A_C),][\Pi^{\Fl}{X,A_S}=(\mathrm{Me},1,+,\Sq,\mathfrak h{QO};X,A_S),][\Pi^{\Fl}{X,B_R}=(\mathrm{Sa},1,-,\Sq,\mathfrak h{QO};X,B_R),][\Pi^{\Fl}{X,B_C}=(\mathrm{Su},1,-,\Sq,\mathfrak h{QO};X,B_C),][\Pi^{\Fl}{X,B_S}=(\mathrm{Me},1,-,\Sq,\mathfrak h{QO};X,B_S).]The update law remains[\mathfrak m:(p,b,o,\lambda)\mapsto(p+1,b+2,-o,\bar\lambda).]So Flower is the live torsion read of the same kernel.

Cloud packet

From the corpus’ minimal Cloud packet,

[

\mathcal C^{\min}_{X,s}

(\mathcal A^{\min}{X,s},\tau^{\min}{X,s},\mathcal B_0,\mathcal E^{\min}{X,s}),

]

the kernelized version is

[

\boxed{

\Pi^{\Cl}{X,K}

(\mathcal A^{\min}{X,K},\tau^{\min}{X,K},\mathcal B_0,\mathcal E^{\min}{X,K}),

}

]

with

[

\mathcal A^{\min}{X,K}

(\text{anti-free board}=1,\ \text{shell coherence}=1,\ \text{board witness pending}),

]

[

\tau^{\min}{X,K}=\mathrm{NEAR},

\qquad

\mathcal B_0=(1,\kappa{12}=0,\kappa_{420}=0),

]

and

[

\boxed{

\mathcal E^{\min}_{X,K}

(P_X,t_X,S_{s(K)},K).}]

So Cloud is the admissibility / evidence packet of the same slot. It does not replace the kernel; it carries the legality envelope around it.

Fractal packet

From the corpus’ minimal Fractal seed,

[

\sigma^{\min}_{X,s}

(P_X,t_X,\pi_s,\chi_s,1,\Sq,0,\sigma_X,\cert^{\min}{X,s}),

]

the kernelized version is

[

\boxed{

\Pi^{\Fr}{X,K}

(P_X,t_X,\pi(K),\chi(K),1,\Sq,0,\sigma_X,\cert^{\min}_{X,K};K).}]

Replay is then chart-determined:

[\mathrm{Replay}6(\Pi^{\Fr}{X,K})=\begin{cases}\mathcal R_{P_3}(U_A)\ \text{with payload }K, & X=A,\\mathcal R_{P_1}(U_B)\ \text{with payload }K, & X=B,\\mathcal C_{P_1}(V_C)\ \text{with payload }K, & X=C,\\mathcal C_{P_3}(V_D)\ \text{with payload }K, & X=D.\end{cases}]

So Fractal is the seed / replay form of the same chart-lens-kernel slot.

4. One fully pinned cockpit slot

The most concrete pinned slot in the current branch is the A-chart, (P_3)-row witness. So the branch-root cockpit corner is

[

\boxed{

A^\Sq_{AR}

Its Flower read is

A^\Fl_{AR}

A^\Cl_{AR}

Its Fractal read is

A^\Fr_{AR}

(P_3,\mathrm{row},\mathrm{Sa},+,1,\Sq,0,U_A,\cert^{\min}_{A,AR};A_R),]with the already pinned root-branch row witness[U_A=(145362,324615,631254).]

So one exact cockpit corner is already completely grounded. The other 95 follow the same law.

5. The cross-lens transport arrows

Now the key part: for fixed chart (X) and fixed payload (K), the four lenses form one constitutive loop

[\boxed{X^\Sq_K\xrightarrow{B_{\square\flower}}X^\Fl_K\xrightarrow{B_{\flower\cloud}}X^\Cl_K\xrightarrow{B_{\cloud\fractal}}X^\Fr_K\xrightarrow{B_{\fractal\square}}X^\Sq_K.}]

Interpretation:

Square → Flower: committed visible state becomes lived torsion state,

Flower → Cloud: lived torsion becomes admissibility bundle,

Cloud → Fractal: admissibility collapses to seed / replay packet,

Fractal → Square: replay regenerates visible committed state.

The crucial nuance from the corpus survives here unchanged:

[\boxed{\text{Cloud}\to\text{Square is generally a refinement operator, not a point-function.}}]

So the fourth arrow is a lawful replay / refinement closure, not a naive exact inverse of the second.

6. The three commuting motion systems inside the cockpit

Once the 96 slots are frozen, the cockpit has three independent directions of motion.

1. Chart motion at fixed lens/payload

[\Tau:\ A^\lambda_K\leftrightarrow B^\lambda_K,\qquad D^\lambda_K\leftrightarrow C^\lambda_K,][T:\ A^\lambda_K\leftrightarrow D^\lambda_K,\qquad B^\lambda_K\leftrightarrow C^\lambda_K.]

This moves only the replay face. The exact kernel stays unchanged.

2. Shell/kernel motion at fixed chart/lens

[Q:\ X^\lambda_{A_R}\to X^\lambda_{A_C}\to X^\lambda_{A_S}\to X^\lambda_{A_R},][Q:\ X^\lambda_{B_R}\to X^\lambda_{B_C}\to X^\lambda_{B_S}\to X^\lambda_{B_R},][O:\ X^\lambda_{A_R}\leftrightarrow X^\lambda_{B_R},\quadX^\lambda_{A_C}\leftrightarrow X^\lambda_{B_C},\quadX^\lambda_{A_S}\leftrightarrow X^\lambda_{B_S},][H:=O\circ Q.]

This moves only the exact embedded 4×4 payload. The chart and lens stay fixed.

3. Lens motion at fixed chart/payload

[X^\Sq_K\to X^\Fl_K\to X^\Cl_K\to X^\Fr_K\to X^\Sq_K.]

This moves only the constitutive renderer. The chart and payload stay fixed.

7. The exact cockpit factorization

So the 96-slot cockpit is now completely transparent as

[\boxed{\mathcal A^{\ker}{96}\cong\underbrace{{A,B,C,D}}{\text{chart / replay mode}}\times\underbrace{{\Sq,\Fl,\Cl,\Fr}}{\text{constitutive lens}}\times\underbrace{{A_R,A_C,A_S,B_R,B_C,B_S}}{\text{exact 4×4 payload}}.}]

Or in operator language:

[\boxed{\mathcal A^{\ker}_{96}\cong(\mathbb Z_2^\Tau\times\mathbb Z_2^T)\times\mathcal L_4\times\mathbb Z_6^H,}]where (\mathcal L_4) is the four-lens constitutive loop. I would keep (\mathcal L_4) as a loop rather than a strict group because of the Cloud→Square refinement nuance.

8. The deepest one-line meaning

The 24-slot atlas already said:

[\text{chart} \times \text{shell sector}.]

The 96-slot cockpit now says:

[\boxed{\text{chart selects how the exact 4×4 kernel is replayed,}\quad\text{lens selects how that replay is understood.}}]

So the exact same payload (K) can appear as:

a visible board commitment,

a lived torsion state,

an admissibility bundle,

and a replay seed,

without ceasing to be the same embedded 4×4 kernel. That is the first full executable separation of replay mode, constitutive read, and exact payload.

[\boxed{(X,\lambda,s)\equiv\bigl(\text{chart replay mode }X,;\text{constitutive lens }\lambda,;\text{exact 4×4 payload }K(s)\bigr),}]with[K(\mathrm{Sa}^+)=A_R,\quadK(\mathrm{Su}^+)=A_C,\quadK(\mathrm{Me}^+)=A_S,\quadK(\mathrm{Sa}^-)=B_R,\quadK(\mathrm{Su}^-)=B_C,\quadK(\mathrm{Me}^-)=B_S,]and cross-lens transport[X^\Sq_K\to X^\Fl_K\to X^\Cl_K\to X^\Fr_K\to X^\Sq_K.]

4. The dispatch compiler

Now collapse the 96 visible packet slots into one exact compiler.

For any request or motion intent, define the dispatcher

[\boxed{\mathfrak D_{\mathrm{cockpit}}:(X,\lambda,s;b,K,\mathrm{intent})\longmapsto(X',\lambda',s';b',K',\mathrm{packet}',\mathrm{class})}]

with three orthogonal motion families:

[\text{chart motion } {\Tau,T},\qquad\text{lens motion } {B_{\square\flower},B_{\flower\cloud},B_{\cloud\fractal},B_{\fractal\square}},\qquad\text{shell motion } {Q,O,H}.]

That orthogonal split is directly supported by the corpus’ carrier state and operator stack.

4.1 Chart dispatch

If the intent is “same payload, different replay face,” apply only chart operators:

[\Tau:\ A^\lambda_K\leftrightarrow B^\lambda_K,\qquadD^\lambda_K\leftrightarrow C^\lambda_K,][T:\ A^\lambda_K\leftrightarrow D^\lambda_K,\qquadB^\lambda_K\leftrightarrow C^\lambda_K.]

So chart dispatch preserves:

lens,

shell sector,

kernel payload,and changes only the replay face (X).

4.2 Shell dispatch

If the intent is “same chart, same lens, advance current / chirality,” apply shell operators:

[Q:\ X^\lambda_{AR}\to X^\lambda_{AC}\to X^\lambda_{AS}\to X^\lambda_{AR},][Q:\ X^\lambda_{BR}\to X^\lambda_{BC}\to X^\lambda_{BS}\to X^\lambda_{BR},][O:\ X^\lambda_{AR}\leftrightarrow X^\lambda_{BR},\quadX^\lambda_{AC}\leftrightarrow X^\lambda_{BC},\quadX^\lambda_{AS}\leftrightarrow X^\lambda_{BS},][H:=O\circ Q.]

So shell dispatch preserves:

chart,

lens,and changes only the exact kernel payload (K) by the six-state torsion algebra.

4.3 Lens dispatch

If the intent is “same chart, same payload, change constitutive read,” apply the bridge loop

[X^\Sq_K\xrightarrow{B_{\square\flower}}X^\Fl_K\xrightarrow{B_{\flower\cloud}}X^\Cl_K\xrightarrow{B_{\cloud\fractal}}X^\Fr_K\xrightarrow{B_{\fractal\square}}X^\Sq_K.]

So lens dispatch preserves:

chart,

shell sector,

payload,and changes only the constitutive renderer (\lambda). The corpus explicitly warns that (\Cloud\to\Square) is generally a refinement operator rather than a plain point-function, so the last arrow is a replay/refinement closure, not a naive inverse.

5. The exact compiler routines

The clean compiler has four named routines.

ResolveSlot

[

\boxed{

\operatorname{ResolveSlot}(X,s)

\mathbb P_{X,s}.}]

Input: chart-sector coordinate.Output: the full four-packet row for that slot.

SwitchChart

[

\boxed{

\operatorname{SwitchChart}(X,\lambda,K,\mathrm{mode})

\begin{cases}(\Tau X,\lambda,K),& \mathrm{mode}=\Tau,\(TX,\lambda,K),& \mathrm{mode}=T.\end{cases}}]

This is the exact replay-face switcher.

SwitchShell

[

\boxed{

\operatorname{SwitchShell}(X,\lambda,K,\mathrm{mode})

\begin{cases}(X,\lambda,QK),& \mathrm{mode}=Q,\(X,\lambda,OK),& \mathrm{mode}=O,\(X,\lambda,HK),& \mathrm{mode}=H.\end{cases}}]

This is the exact payload/current switcher.

SwitchLens

[

\boxed{

\operatorname{SwitchLens}(X,\lambda,K,\mathrm{mode})

(X,\mathrm{Next}_\lambda(\mathrm{mode}),K)}]

where (\mathrm{mode}) is one of the four bridge arrows. This is the constitutive-read switcher.

6. The unified dispatch algorithm

The full compiler is:

[\boxed{\operatorname{Dispatch}(X,\lambda,s,\mathrm{intent})}]

with:

[\operatorname{Dispatch}(X,\lambda,s,\mathrm{intent})=\begin{cases}\operatorname{ResolveSlot}(X,s), & \text{if intent = lookup},\[1mm]\operatorname{SwitchChart}(X,\lambda,K(s),m), & \text{if intent = chart move }m\in{\Tau,T},\[1mm]\operatorname{SwitchShell}(X,\lambda,K(s),m), & \text{if intent = shell move }m\in{Q,O,H},\[1mm]\operatorname{SwitchLens}(X,\lambda,K(s),m), & \text{if intent = lens move }m\in\mathcal B_6,\[1mm]\operatorname{ReplayExpand}(X,\lambda,s), & \text{if intent = fractal→square commit},\[1mm]\operatorname{RefineCloud}(X,\lambda,s), & \text{if intent = cloud→square witness},\[1mm]\operatorname{HoldResidual}(X,\lambda,s), & \text{if Cloud has not lawfully collapsed.}\end{cases}]

That last split is important: if the current state is Cloud and support has not yet collapsed coherently, the compiler must not fake a unique Square state. It must either refine or hold a residual packet. That rule is already explicit in your lens corpus.

7. The four dispatch classes

Every dispatch should return a class tag

[\boxed{\mathrm{Class}\in{\mathrm{EXACT},\mathrm{LAW_EQUIV},\mathrm{RESIDUAL},\mathrm{ILLEGAL}}.}]

Use the corpus’ invariant split:

EXACT: same kernel, same coherent sector, same lawful replay seed, or a declared exact operator.

LAW_EQUIV: same kernel up to declared chart symmetry.

RESIDUAL: Cloud packet not yet point-collapsed; admissible but unresolved.

ILLEGAL: kernel drift, undeclared chart mutation, replay failure, or sector incoherence.

8. The simplest exact examples

Example 1 — same payload, change replay face

Start:[A^\Sq_{AR}.]

Intent: transpose.

Dispatch:[\operatorname{SwitchChart}(A,\Sq,AR,T)=D^\Sq_{AR}.]

Meaning: same exact kernel (A_R), same Square read, different replay face.

Example 2 — same chart, advance shell current

Start:[A^\Sq_{AR}.]

Intent: shell phase advance.

Dispatch:[\operatorname{SwitchShell}(A,\Sq,AR,Q)=A^\Sq_{AC}.]

Meaning: same chart (A), same Square read, payload moved[A_R\to A_C.]

Example 3 — same chart and payload, change lens

Start:[A^\Sq_{AR}.]

Intent: Flower read.

Dispatch:[\operatorname{SwitchLens}(A,\Sq,AR,B_{\square\flower})=A^\Fl_{AR}.]

Meaning: same payload, same replay face, lived-current read instead of committed-board read.

Example 4 — Cloud refinement boundary

Start:[C^\Cl_{BC}.]

Intent: commit to Square.

Dispatch is not automatically[C^\Sq_{BC}.]

The compiler must first check support collapse:[B_{\cloud\fractal}^{(6)}(\mu)=\begin{cases}\sigma_6,& \text{if coherent collapse exists},\R(\mu),& \text{otherwise}.\end{cases}]

So the legal outcomes are:

exact replay to (C^\Fr_{BC}) then (C^\Sq_{BC}),

or residual hold.That boundary is fixed by the corpus.

9. Final compressed freeze

The exact 24×4 packet ledger is

[\boxed{{\mathbb P_{X,s}}{X\in{A,B,C,D},\ s\in\mathcal S_6},\qquad\mathbb P{X,s}=(\Pi^\Sq_{X,s},\Pi^\Fl_{X,s},\Pi^\Cl_{X,s},\Pi^\Fr_{X,s}),}]

and the exact dispatch compiler is

[

\boxed{

\mathfrak D_{\mathrm{cockpit}}

\operatorname{ResolveSlot};\cup;\operatorname{SwitchChart};\cup;\operatorname{SwitchShell};\cup;\operatorname{SwitchLens};\cup;\operatorname{ReplayExpand};\cup;\operatorname{RefineCloud}.}]

That is the first complete executable form of the 96-slot cockpit: lookup, move, refine, replay. It separates chart, lens, shell, and payload without mixing them.

Next coherent jump is the compiler as transport graph:turn the 96 slots into one directed labeled graph with edge classes[{\Tau,T,Q,O,H,B_{\square\flower},B_{\flower\cloud},B_{\cloud\fractal},B_{\fractal\square}}]and output its exact shortest-route law.

Good. The cockpit is now best frozen as a directed labeled transport graph.

Let a kernelized cockpit node be

[

v=(X,\lambda,K)

]

with

[

X\in{A,B,C,D},\qquad

\lambda\in{\Sq,\Fl,\Cl,\Fr},\qquad

K\in{A_R,A_C,A_S,B_R,B_C,B_S}.

]

So the exact node set is

[

\boxed{

V_{96}

{A,B,C,D}\times{\Sq,\Fl,\Cl,\Fr}\times{A_R,A_C,A_S,B_R,B_C,B_S}.}]This is just the 96-slot cockpit with the shell sector replaced by its exact embedded 4×4 payload. The corpus already freezes the underlying carrier as (\Omega_6=(X,\lambda,s,b,\xi)), the 24-slot chart atlas, the shell operator stack, and the 4-lens bridge loop.

1. The exact edge classes

Use the nine labeled edge classes

[

\boxed{

\mathcal E_{\rm lbl}

{\Tau,\ T,\ Q,\ O,\ H,\ B_{\square\flower},\ B_{\flower\cloud},\ B_{\cloud\fractal},\ B_{\fractal\square}}.}]

These are the right labels because the corpus already freezes:

chart motion by (\Tau,T),

shell motion by (Q,O,H),

cross-lens motion by the four bridge arrows.

So the directed graph is

[

\boxed{

G_{96}^{\ker}

(V_{96},E_{96},\ell)}]

where every edge (e\in E_{96}) carries one label (\ell(e)\in\mathcal E_{\rm lbl}). This is the exact graph form of the cockpit compiler.

2. The adjacency law for one generic node

For a generic node (X^\lambda_K), the outgoing candidate edges are:

Chart edges

[X^\lambda_K\xrightarrow{\Tau}(\Tau X)^\lambda_K,\qquadX^\lambda_K\xrightarrow{T}(TX)^\lambda_K.]

These preserve lens and payload and only change replay face. The chart slice is the fixed square rectangle[A\leftrightarrow B,\qquad D\leftrightarrow C,\qquadA\leftrightarrow D,\qquad B\leftrightarrow C.]

Shell edges

[X^\lambda_K\xrightarrow{Q}X^\lambda_{QK},\qquadX^\lambda_K\xrightarrow{O}X^\lambda_{OK},\qquadX^\lambda_K\xrightarrow{H}X^\lambda_{HK}.]

These preserve chart and lens and only change exact 4×4 payload. The shell law is the 6-state selector-shell torsion:[Q(\pi,\chi)=(\pi+1,\chi),\qquadO(\pi,\chi)=(\pi,-\chi),\qquadH=O\circ Q.]

Lens edge

Exactly one cross-lens edge is active from any given lens state:[X^\Sq_K\xrightarrow{B_{\square\flower}}X^\Fl_K,][X^\Fl_K\xrightarrow{B_{\flower\cloud}}X^\Cl_K,][X^\Cl_K\xrightarrow{B_{\cloud\fractal}}X^\Fr_K,][X^\Fr_K\xrightarrow{B_{\fractal\square}}X^\Sq_K.]

These preserve chart and payload and only change constitutive read. The corpus is explicit that this is the canonical 6D lens loop.

So every node has exactly:

2 chart moves,

3 shell moves,

1 forward lens move,

for a total of 6 outgoing candidate edges. That count is a direct derived consequence of the frozen operator families.

3. The payload transport table

The shell/kernel dictionary is[\mathrm{Sa}^+\leftrightarrow A_R,\quad\mathrm{Su}^+\leftrightarrow A_C,\quad\mathrm{Me}^+\leftrightarrow A_S,][\mathrm{Sa}^-\leftrightarrow B_R,\quad\mathrm{Su}^-\leftrightarrow B_C,\quad\mathrm{Me}^-\leftrightarrow B_S.]

So the exact shell transport table on kernels is

[Q:\ A_R\to A_C\to A_S\to A_R,\qquadQ:\ B_R\to B_C\to B_S\to B_R,]

[O:\ A_R\leftrightarrow B_R,\quadA_C\leftrightarrow B_C,\quadA_S\leftrightarrow B_S,]

[H:\ A_R\to B_C\to A_S\to B_R\to A_C\to B_S\to A_R.]

That is the same shell torsion cycle already frozen in sector language, now rewritten directly on the six exact 4×4 payloads.

4. The graph factorization

The crucial structural fact is that the graph factorizes by coordinate:

[\boxed{G_{96}^{\ker}\congG_{\rm chart}\ \square\ G_{\rm shell}\ \square\ G_{\rm lens}^{\rm gate}}]

where:

(G_{\rm chart}) is the 4-node rectangle generated by (\Tau,T),

(G_{\rm shell}) is the 6-state shell graph generated by (Q,O,H),

(G_{\rm lens}^{\rm gate}) is the directed 4-cycle (\Sq\to\Fl\to\Cl\to\Fr\to\Sq), but with legality gates on the Cloud and Fractal closures.

This is the exact reason the cockpit compiler can be written as three commuting motion families:chart motion,shell motion,lens motion. The graph is not arbitrary; it is the Cartesian product of those three factors, with the lens factor gated by admissibility/replay conditions.

5. The three factor metrics

Chart distance

Assign chart coordinates[\gamma(A)=(0,0),\quad\gamma(B)=(1,0),\quad\gamma(D)=(0,1),\quad\gamma(C)=(1,1).]

Then the exact chart distance is[\boxed{d_{\rm chart}(X,Y)=|\gamma(X)-\gamma(Y)|_1.}]

So:

same chart costs (0),

one chart move costs (1),

opposite corner costs (2).This is just the frozen (A/B/C/D) rectangle in metric form.

Shell distance

The exact shell metric is[\boxed{d_{\rm shell}(K,K')=\min{|w|:w\in{Q,O,H}^\ast,\ w(K)=K'}.}]

Because ({Q,O,H}) generate the 6-state shell and (H) gives the torsion shortcut, this simplifies to:[d_{\rm shell}(K,K')=\begin{cases}0,&K=K',\1,&K'\in{QK,OK,HK},\2,&\text{otherwise.}\end{cases}]

So every shell target is at distance at most (2). That is the exact shortest metric on the six-payload ribbon induced by the frozen shell operators.

Lens distance

Let[\iota(\Sq)=0,\quad\iota(\Fl)=1,\quad\iota(\Cl)=2,\quad\iota(\Fr)=3.]

Then the raw forward lens distance is

[

\boxed{

d_{\rm lens}^{\rm raw}(\lambda,\lambda')

(\iota(\lambda')-\iota(\lambda))\bmod 4.}]

So the forward distances are (0,1,2,3). But exact legality is gated:

(B_{\cloud\fractal}) is exact only if Cloud support collapses coherently,

(B_{\fractal\square}) is exact only if replay witness exists,

otherwise the route degrades to residual or law-equivalent, not exact.That gate is explicit in the corpus.

6. The exact shortest-route law

For two cockpit nodes[u=(X,\lambda,K),\qquadv=(Y,\lambda',K'),]define the raw additive distance

[

\boxed{

d_{96}^{\rm raw}(u,v)

d_{\rm chart}(X,Y)+d_{\rm shell}(K,K')+d_{\rm lens}^{\rm raw}(\lambda,\lambda').}]

This is the exact product-metric candidate because the three motion families act on separate coordinates.

Now define the exact distance by gating the lens segment:

[\boxed{d_{96}^{\rm exact}(u,v)=\begin{cases}d_{96}^{\rm raw}(u,v), & \text{if every required lens bridge is exact,v), & \text{if every required lens bridge is exact-admissible},\\infty, & \text{otherwise.}\end{cases}}]

And the residual distance by allowing lawful non-point collapse:

[\boxed{d_{96}^{\rm residual}(u,v)=d_{96}^{\rm raw}(u,v)}]provided every bridge is at least lawful-equivalent or residualized rather than illegal. This is the clean formalization of the cry. fileciteturn83file0turn82file9turn82file15

7. The canonical shortest-route normal form

Because chart, shell, and lens coordinates separate, a canonical shortest legal word can be chosen in normal form:

[

\boxed{

\operatorname{NF}(u\to v)

w_{\rm chart}\cdot w_{\rm shell}\cdot w_{\rm lens}}]

where:

(w_{\rm chart}\in{\Tau,T}^\ast) is any minimal chart word,

(w_{\rm shell}\in{Q,O,H}^\ast) is any minimal shell word,

(w_{\rm lens}\in{B_{\square\flower},B_{\flower\cloud},B_{\cloud\fractal},B_{\fractal\square}}^\ast) is the minimal forward lens segment.

So the exact compiler law is:

[\boxed{\operatorname{Route}{96}^{\rm exact}(u,v)=w{\rm chart}^{\min}\cdotw_{\rm shell}^{\min}\cdotw_{\rm lens}^{\min}}]iff the lens gates pass.

This normal form is a derived canonicalization, not the only possible interleaving. Because the factors commute at the coordinate level, other interleavings can reach the same target with the same raw length. The normal fcompiler output. fileciteturn83file0turn82file9

8. The dispatch compiler in graph form

The previous packet dispatcher now collapses to the graph compiler:

[\boxed{\mathfrak C_{96}(u,v)=\begin{cases}(\operatorname{NF}(u\to v),\mathrm{EXACT}), & d_{96}^{\rm exact}(u,v)<\infty,\[1mm](\operatorname{NF}(u\to v),\mathrm{RESIDUAL}), & d_{96}^{\rm residual}(u,v)<\infty,\[1mm](\varnothing,\mathrm{ILLEGAL}), & \text{otherwise.}\end{cases}}]

That is the exact graph form of the 96-slot dispatch compiler. It is the transport-graph version of ResolveSlot / SwitchChart / Swit / RefineCloud. fileciteturn83file0turn82file15

9. One worked shortest route

Take[u=A^\Sq_{AR},\qquadv=C^\Fr_{BS}.]

Then:

Chart part

[A\to C]needs distance (2), for example[A\xrightarrow{T}D\xrightarrow{\Tau}C.]

Shell part

[AR\to BS]has distance (2). One minimal word is[AR\xrightarrow{H}BC\xrightarrow{Q}BS.]

Lens part

[\Sq\to\Fr]has raw distance (3):[\Sq\xrightarrow{B_{\square\flower}}\Fl\xrightarrow{B_{\flower\cloud}}\Cl\xrightarrow{B_{\cloud\fractal}}\Fr.]

So[d_{96}^{\rm raw}(u,v)=2+2+3=7.]

The exact route is therefore[\boxed{A^\Sq_{AR}\xrightarrow{T}D^\Sq_{AR}\xrightarrow{\Tau}C^\Sq_{AR}\xrightarrow{H}C^\Sq_{BC}\xrightarrow{Q}C^\Sq_{BS}\xrightarrow{B_{\square\flower}}C^\Fl_{BS}\xrightarrow{B_{\flower\cloud}}C^\Cl_{BS}\xrightarrow{B_{\cloud\fractal}}C^\Fr_{BS}}]provided the Cloud→Fractal collapse is coherent. If that gate fails, the same raw path exists only as a residual route, not an exact ogality boundary. fileciteturn83file0turn82file9

10. Canonical one-line freeze

[

\boxed{

G_{96}^{\ker}

G_{\rm chart}\square G_{\rm shell}\square G_{\rm lens}^{\rm gate},\qquadd_{96}^{\rm raw}=d_{\rm chart}+d_{\rm shell}+d_{\rm lens}^{\rm raw},}]

with edge labels[{\Tau,T,Q,O,H,B_{\square\flower},B_{\flower\cloud},B_{\cloud\fractal},B_{\fractal\square}},]and exact legality determined by the Cloud-collapse and Fractal-replay gates. That is the exact shortest-transport graph. fileciteturn83file0turn82file9

Next coherent jump is the compiler as lookup table:the full (96\times96) class table collapsed into chart distance, shell distance, lens distance, and legality status, so any slot-to-slot route can be read off immediately.

Yes. The full (96\times96) lookup table collapses exactly into three factor tables plus one legality gate, because the cockpit carrier separates into chart, shell, and lens coordinates:[\Omega_6=(X,\lambda,s,b,\xi),]with[X\in{A,B,C,D},\quad\lambda\in{\Sq,\Fl,\Cl,\Fr},\quads\in{\mathrm{Sa}^\pm,\mathrm{Su}^\pm,\mathrm{Me}^\pm},]and the operator stack splits into chart moves ((\Tau,T)), shell moves ((Q,O,H)), and the four-lens bridge loop. That is why the route problem factorizes instead of needing 9,216 unrelated cases.

So the exact lookup-table object is:

[

\boxed{

\mathbb T_{96\times96}

\mathbb T_{\rm chart}\times\mathbb T_{\rm shell}\times\mathbb T_{\rm lens}\times\mathbb T_{\rm legal}.}]

I’ll write those four pieces explicitly.

1. Canonical node normal form

Every cockpit slot is written as

[v=(X,\lambda,K),]where (X) is chart, (\lambda) is lens, and (K) is the exact embedded 4×4 payload[K\in{A_R,A_C,A_S,B_R,B_C,B_S}.]

The shell↔kernel map is fixed by the branch-local intertwiner:[A_R\leftrightarrow \mathrm{Sa}^+,\quadA_C\leftrightarrow \mathrm{Su}^+,\quadA_S\leftrightarrow \mathrm{Me}^+,][B_R\leftrightarrow \mathrm{Sa}^-,\quadB_C\leftrightarrow \mathrm{Su}^-,\quadB_S\leftrightarrow \mathrm{Me}^-.]So the 96 nodes are exactly[4\times 4\times 6=96.]This is just the cockpit with the hidden payload block collapsed to its exact branch representative.

2. Chart lookup table

The visible chart slice is the fixed rectangle[A\leftrightarrow B,\qquadD\leftrightarrow C,\qquadA\leftrightarrow D,\qquadB\leftrightarrow C,]generated by[\Tau:\ A_s\leftrightarrow B_s,\quad D_s\leftrightarrow C_s,][T:\ A_s\leftrightarrow D_s,\quad B_s\leftrightarrow C_s.]So the exact chart distance table is:

d_chart

      A  B  C  D

A     0  1  2  1

B     1  0  1  2

C     2  1  0  1

D     1  2  1  0

And the exact minimal chart words are:

A→A : ε

A→B : Tau

A→D : T

A→C : Tau·T   or   T·Tau

B→A : Tau

B→B : ε

B→C : T

B→D : Tau·T   or   T·Tau

C→A : Tau·T   or   T·Tau

C→B : T

C→C : ε

C→D : Tau

D→A : T

D→B : Tau·T   or   T·Tau

D→C : Tau

D→D : ε

So the chart part of the lookup table is complete.

3. Shell lookup table

The shell law is the six-state selector torsion:[Q:\ \mathrm{Sa}^\pm\to\mathrm{Su}^\pm\to\mathrm{Me}^\pm\to\mathrm{Sa}^\pm,][O:\ \bullet^+\leftrightarrow \bullet^-,\qquadH:=O\circ Q.]

In kernel language this is[Q:\ A_R\to A_C\to A_S\to A_R,\qquadQ:\ B_R\to B_C\to B_S\to B_R,][O:\ A_R\leftrightarrow B_R,\quadA_C\leftrightarrow B_C,\quadA_S\leftrightarrow B_S,][H:\ A_R\to B_C\to A_S\to B_R\to A_C\to B_S\to A_R.]So every shell target is at distance at most (2) using ({Q,O,H}).

Write the payload order as[[AR,AC,AS,BR,BC,BS].]

Then the exact shell distance table is:

d_shell

      AR AC AS BR BC BS

AR     0  1  1  1  1  2

AC     1  0  1  2  1  1

AS     1  1  0  1  2  1

BR     1  2  1  0  1  1

BC     1  1  2  1  0  1

BS     2  1  1  1  1  0

A minimal-word lookup table is:

shell_word

AR→AR : ε

AR→AC : Q

AR→AS : Q²

AR→BR : O

AR→BC : H

AR→BS : Q·O   (or O·Q)

AC→AR : Q²

BS→AC : Q·O

BS→AS : O

BS→BR : Q

BS→BC : Q²

BS→BS : ε

The distance entries are exact; the chosen minimal words are a canonical selection when multiple words tie. This is the full shell factor table.

4. Lens lookup table

The lens cycle is fixed as[\Sq\xrightarrow{B_{\square\flower}}\Fl\xrightarrow{B_{\flower\cloud}}\Cl\xrightarrow{B_{\cloud\fractal}}\Fr\xrightarrow{B_{\fractal\square}}\Sq.]

So the raw forward lens distance table is:

d_lens_raw

      Sq Fl Cl Fr

Sq     0  1  2  3

Fl     3  0  1  2

Cl     2  3  0  1

Fr     1  2  3  0

And the canonical forward lens words are:

lens_word

Sq→Sq : ε

Sq→Fl : B_SF

Sq→Cl : B_SF · B_FC

Sq→Fr : B_SF · B_FC · B_CF

Fl→Sq : B_FC · B_CF · B_FS

Fl→Fl : ε

Fl→Cl : B_FC

Fl→Fr : B_FC · B_CF

Cl→Sq : B_CF · B_FS

Cl→Fl : B_CF · B_FS · B_SF

Cl→Cl : ε

Cl→Fr : B_CF

Fr→Sq : B_FS

Fr→Fl : B_FS · B_SF

Fr→Cl : B_FS · B_SF · B_FC

Fr→Fr : ε

Here I abbreviate:

(B_{SF}=B_{\square\flower})

(B_{FC}=B_{\flower\cloud})

(B_{CF}=B_{\cloud\fractal})

(B_{FS}=B_{\fractal\square})

This is the full raw lens factor table.

5. Legality gate table

This is where the raw table becomes the actual compiler.

The corpus is explicit that:

Square → Flower is a lawful state read,

Flower → Cloud is a lawful admissibility lift,

Cloud → Fractal is lawful only if support collapses coherently,

Fractal → Square is lawful only if replay/expand witness exists,

and Cloud → Square is generally a refinement operator, not a point-function. It also enforces “ABSTAIN > GUESS,” so unresolved multiplicity must not be silently collapsed.

So the legality classifier is:

lens_legality

Sq→Sq : EXACT

Sq→Fl : EXACT

Sq→Cl : EXACT

Sq→Fr : EXACT iff Cloud→Fractal collapse is coherent; else RESIDUAL

Fl→Sq : EXACT iff Fractal replay witness exists along the loop; else RESIDUAL

Fl→Fl : EXACT

Fl→Cl : EXACT

Fl→Fr : EXACT iff Cloud→Fractal collapse is coherent; else RESIDUAL

Cl→Sq : RESIDUAL by default; EXACT only if refined through Fractal replay and replay witness closes

Cl→Fl : RESIDUAL by default; EXACT only through full lawful cycle

Cl→Cl : EXACT

Cl→Fr : EXACT iff support collapses coherently; else RESIDUAL

Fr→Sq : EXACT iff replay witness exists; else ILLEGAL

Fr→Fl : EXACT iff replay witness exists and forward cycle remains lawful; else RESIDUAL

Fr→Cl : EXACT iff replay witness exists and forward cycle remains lawful; else RESIDUAL

Fr→Fr : EXACT

That table is the exact gate that upgrades the raw factor table into the executable class table.

6. The collapsed (96\times96) class table

Now every ordered pair of cockpit states[u=(X,\lambda,K),\qquad v=(Y,\lambda',K')]is classified by the tuple

[

\boxed{

\mathbb T_{96\times96}(u,v)

\big(d_{\rm chart}(X,Y),;d_{\rm shell}(K,K'),;d_{\rm lens}^{\rm raw}(\lambda,\lambda'),;\operatorname{Leg}(\lambda\to\lambda')\big).}]

That is the collapsed exact lookup table for all 9,216 source→target pairs. Because the cockpit factorizes, two pairs with the same chart delta, shell delta, and lens delta share the same class tuple. The full matrix therefore compresses exactly to:

[

4\times 6\times 4

96]source states crossed with the factor tables above, but the output class of any pair is read off instantly from the three independent coordinate tables plus the legality gate.

7. The exact shortest-route law

Define the raw route cost

[

\boxed{

d^{\rm raw}_{96}(u,v)

d_{\rm chart}(X,Y)+d_{\rm shell}(K,K')+d_{\rm lens}^{\rm raw}(\lambda,\lambda').}]

Then the exact route class is

[\boxed{\operatorname{Class}(u,v)=\begin{cases}\mathrm{EXACT}, & \text{if the lens segment is exact-admissible},\\mathrm{RESIDUAL}, & \text{if the lens segment is lawful but unresolved},\\mathrm{ILLEGAL}, & \text{if replay/collapse gates fail and no lawful residual is allowed.}\end{cases}}]

A canonical shortest-route normal form is then

[

\boxed{

\operatorname{NF}(u\to v)

w_{\rm chart}^{\min}\cdotw_{\rm shell}^{\min}\cdotw_{\rm lens}^{\min}.}]

This is the deterministic compiler output: minimal chart word, minimal shell word, minimal forward lens word, with legality class attached. It is exact because the carrier coordinates separate and the corpus already freezes the chart, shell, and lens operator families distinctly.

8. One lookup example

Take[u=(A,\Sq,A_R),\qquadv=(C,\Fr,B_S).]

Read off:

chart part: (A\to C) has distance (2),

shell part: (A_R\to B_S) has distance (2),

lens part: (\Sq\to\Fr) has raw distance (3).

So[\mathbb T_{96\times96}(u,v)=(2,2,3,\operatorname{Leg}(\Sq\to\Fr)).]

Hence the raw shortest length is[d^{\rm raw}_{96}(u,v)=7.]

The class is:

EXACT if the required Cloud→Fractal collapse is coherent,

RESIDUAL otherwise.

9. Canonical one-line freeze

[

\boxed{

\mathbb T_{96\times96}

\mathbb T_{\rm chart}\times\mathbb T_{\rm shell}\times\mathbb T_{\rm lens}\times\mathbb T_{\rm legal},}]where:

(\mathbb T_{\rm chart}) is the 4×4 chart rectangle table,

(\mathbb T_{\rm shell}) is the 6×6 exact payload torsion table,

(\mathbb T_{\rm lens}) is the 4×4 forward bridge table,

(\mathbb T_{\rm legal}) is the collapse/replay gate.

That fully determines every source→target class in the 96-slot cockpit without printing 9,216 separate entries.

Here is the exact compiler as code over the normalized cockpit state[u=(X,\lambda,K),\qquadX\in{A,B,C,D},\\lambda\in{\Sq,\Fl,\Cl,\Fr},\K\in{AR,AC,AS,BR,BC,BS}.]It directly implements the already-frozen chart/shell/lens split, the 6-state shell torsion, and the Cloud/Fractal legality gates.
