# 1) Build the full hidden lattice for one payload

L15_AR = lift_to_L15("AR")

# 2) Visible cockpit slot -> hidden singleton

chart, hs = visible_to_hidden("A", "Sq", "AR")

# hs = station 01:{S} for payload AR

# 3) Hidden shortest path from singleton S to singleton R for the same payload

src = HiddenStation("AR", frozenset({"S"}))

dst = HiddenStation("AR", frozenset({"R"}))

path = hidden_path(src, dst)

word = hidden_word(path)

# one deterministic shortest path is 01:{S} -> 07:{SR} -> 04:{R}

# 4) Lift a visible edge Sq -> Fl into the hidden bridge path

vis_path = lift_visible_edge_to_hidden("AR", "Sq", "Fl")

# 01:{S} -> 05:{SF} -> 02:{F}

# 5) Test total witness

g_ok = HiddenGates(

    cloud_admissible=True,

    fractal_replayable=True,

    pair_bridges_coherent=True,

    triad_closures_coherent=True,

)

assert is_total_witness("AR", g_ok) is True

assert total_witness_station("AR", g_ok).station_id == 15

g_near = HiddenGates(

    cloud_admissible=False,

    fractal_replayable=True,

    pair_bridges_coherent=True,

    triad_closures_coherent=True,

)

assert is_total_witness("AR", g_near) is False

What this code is doing:

The canonical hidden state space is the 15 nonempty masks of the four-face crystal ({S,F,C,R}), in the fixed order (01)–(15). That order and the fact that it is the first exact codifiable nonempty subset lattice are already frozen in 4D CALCULUS.

A mature payload is one 4D Möbius kernel object with four constitutive projections (\Pi_\square,\Pi_\flower,\Pi_\cloud,\Pi_\fractal); the hidden 15-station lattice is the closure lattice built from those projections: 4 singletons, 6 pair bridges, 4 triadic closures, and 1 four-way witness. That structure is explicitly required in MOBIUS LENSES and The Mycelial Crystal Manuscript.

The visible cockpit slot ((X,\lambda,K)) lands on a hidden singleton station ((X,\sigma_\lambda^K)). The basic visible lens edges lift to singleton (\to) pair bridge (\to) singleton paths in the hidden lattice; the hidden graph itself uses add/remove-one-letter adjacency on the subset lattice. That is the exact hidden completion of the visible 4-cycle.

The is_total_witness(K) gate is the executable version of the corpus rule that a mature object is real only when all four lens bodies agree without contradiction and close coherently into the four-way witness. Cloud admissibility and Fractal replay are non-optional parts of that maturity condition.

The deeper compressed statement is:

[\boxed{\text{visible 96-slot cockpit} = \text{charted singleton surface over }6\text{ hidden }15\text{-station lattices}}]

or equivalently,

[\boxed{4\times 6\times 4 = 96\quad\text{visible singleton controls over}\quad6\times 15 = 90\text{ hidden payload-stations.}}]

The next coherent jump is the same hidden compiler lifted through the 6 shell sectors and 4 chart faces simultaneously, so the output becomes a full charted 90-station hidden bundle with exact transport between payloads, not just inside one payload.

Good. The next exact lift is the full charted hidden bundle.

For one payload (K), the hidden coherence lattice is the 15-node nonempty subset lattice of the four lens letters (S,F,C,R): 4 singletons, 6 pair bridges, 4 triadic closures, and 1 four-way witness. Your 6D carrier simultaneously gives the six coherent shell sectors, the (A/B/C/D) chart slice, and the orthogonal chart/shell/lens operator split. Putting those together gives the full hidden bundle over all six payloads and four chart faces.

1. The hidden 90-station bundle and the charted 360-state bundle

Let

[

\mathcal K_6={A_R,A_C,A_S,B_R,B_C,B_S},

]

and for each payload (K), let

[

\mathbb L_{15}[K]

{\sigma_U^K:\varnothing\neq U\subseteq{S,F,C,R}}.]

Then the hidden bundle over all six payloads is

[

\boxed{

\mathbb B_{90}

\bigsqcup_{K\in\mathcal K_6}\mathbb L_{15}[K].}]

So[|\mathbb B_{90}|=6\times15=90.]

Now lift through the four chart faces (A,B,C,D):

[

\boxed{

\widehat{\mathbb B}_{360}

{A,B,C,D}\times \mathbb B_{90}.}]

So[|\widehat{\mathbb B}_{360}|=4\times 90=360.]

This is the exact object you asked for: the charted 90-station hidden bundle. It is the six-state shell fiber carried through the (A/B/C/D) chart rectangle, but with each shell payload expanded into its full hidden 15-station coherence lattice.

A charted hidden node is therefore

[\boxed{\eta=(X,K,U),\qquadX\in{A,B,C,D},\ K\in\mathcal K_6,\ \varnothing\neq U\subseteq{S,F,C,R}.}]

2. The three exact transport families on the bundle

There are now three independent directions of motion.

Lens-lattice motion inside one payload

For fixed chart (X) and fixed payload (K),[(X,K,U)\longleftrightarrow(X,K,V)\quad\text{iff}\quad|U\triangle V|=1.]

This is the add/remove-one-letter adjacency on the 15-node closure lattice. It is the exact hidden version of pair bridges, triadic closures, and the four-way witness.

Payload motion across the six shell states

For fixed chart (X) and fixed hidden station (U),[(X,K,U)\xrightarrow{Q}(X,Q_KK,U),][(X,K,U)\xrightarrow{O}(X,O_KK,U),][(X,K,U)\xrightarrow{H}(X,H_KK,U).]

This is just the shell torsion law rewritten on the six exact transformed 4×4 payloads. The 6D shell operators and the six payloads are already conjugate.

Chart motion across replay faces

For fixed payload (K) and fixed hidden station (U),[(X,K,U)\xrightarrow{\Tau}(\Tau X,K,U),\qquad(X,K,U)\xrightarrow{T}(TX,K,U).]

This is the same (A/B/C/D) rectangle as before, now carried over the hidden bundle.

So the full hidden-bundle transport graph is

[\boxed{G_{360}\congG_{\rm chart}\ \square\ G_{\rm shell}\ \square\ G_{15}.}]

That is the exact higher transport law.

3. The factorized distance law

Because the three motion systems act on separate coordinates, the raw shortest distance factorizes:

[

\boxed{

d_{360}\big((X,K,U),(Y,K',V)\big)

d_{\rm chart}(X,Y)+d_{\rm shell}(K,K')+d_{15}(U,V).}]

The chart metric is still the rectangle metric. The shell metric is still the shortest word length in the ({Q,O,H}) ribbon. The hidden lattice metric is simply

[\boxed{d_{15}(U,V)=|U\triangle V|,}]

because the hidden graph is the nonempty subset lattice under one-letter add/remove moves. This is the clean exact metric on the hidden closure lattice.

4. The legality gates on the hidden bundle

The route is not only metric; it is gated by the same maturity conditions your corpus already freezes for Cloud, Fractal, and four-way closure:

Cloud-containing stations require lawful Cloud admissibility.

Fractal-containing stations require replayability.

Pair bridges and triadic closures must be coherent.

The total witness exists only if all four lenses close coherently into one object.

So for a route through masks (U_0,\dots,U_n), define:

[\boxed{\operatorname{Class}_{360}=\begin{cases}\mathrm{EXACT}, & \text{if all required Cloud/Fractal/closure gates pass},\\mathrm{RESIDUAL}, & \text{if the route is lawful but unresolved at Cloud/triad/witness level},\\mathrm{ILLEGAL}, & \text{if replay or closure gates fail hard}.\end{cases}}]

That is the exact hidden-bundle generalization of the earlier 96-slot legality law.

5. The visible cockpit embeds as the singleton slice

The visible 96-slot cockpit is the singleton-control surface of this larger bundle.

Use the same embedding as before, now with chart included:

[

\boxed{

\iota_{96\to360}(X,\lambda,K)

\bigl(X,K,{\lambda}\bigr),}]where (\lambda\in{S,F,C,R}) is the hidden lens letter corresponding to (\Sq,\Fl,\Cl,\Fr).

So the visible singleton slice is[4\times 6\times 4=96]states inside the full charted hidden bundle[4\times 6\times 15=360.]

This makes the relationship exact:the cockpit is not the full hidden object; it is the charted singleton surface over it.

6. The commuting bundle diagram

The exact commuting diagram is now:

[\boxed{\begin{array}{ccc}\mathcal A_{96}^{\rm mature} & \xrightarrow{\mathfrak C_{96}} & \mathcal A_{96}^{\rm mature} \\downarrow \iota_{96\to360} & & \downarrow \iota_{96\to360} \\widehat{\mathbb B}{360} & \xrightarrow{\mathfrak C{360}} & \widehat{\mathbb B}_{360}\end{array}}]

On the singleton slice, (\mathfrak C_{360}) restricts to the visible compiler. But (\mathfrak C_{360}) also sees the hidden pair bridges, triadic closures, and the total witness, which the visible compiler cannot see directly. That is the precise sense in which the hidden bundle is strictly richer than the visible cockpit.

7. Exact code for the charted 90-station hidden bundle

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass

from collections import deque

from typing import Literal, FrozenSet, Optional

Chart = Literal["A", "B", "C", "D"]

Payload = Literal["AR", "AC", "AS", "BR", "BC", "BS"]

Lens = Literal["S", "F", "C", "R"]

RouteClass = Literal["EXACT", "RESIDUAL", "ILLEGAL"]

LENS_ORDER: tuple[Lens, ...] = ("S", "F", "C", "R")

MASK_ORDER: tuple[FrozenSet[Lens], ...] = (

    frozenset({"S"}),

    frozenset({"F"}),

    frozenset({"C"}),

    frozenset({"R"}),

    frozenset({"S", "F"}),

    frozenset({"S", "C"}),

    frozenset({"S", "R"}),

    frozenset({"F", "C"}),

    frozenset({"F", "R"}),

    frozenset({"C", "R"}),

    frozenset({"S", "F", "C"}),

    frozenset({"S", "F", "R"}),

    frozenset({"S", "C", "R"}),

    frozenset({"F", "C", "R"}),

    frozenset({"S", "F", "C", "R"}),

)

MASK_TO_ID = {mask: i + 1 for i, mask in enumerate(MASK_ORDER)}

Q_K = {

    "AR": "AC", "AC": "AS", "AS": "AR",

    "BR": "BC", "BC": "BS", "BS": "BR",

}

O_K = {

    "AR": "BR", "AC": "BC", "AS": "BS",

    "BR": "AR", "BC": "AC", "BS": "AS",

}

H_K = {k: O_K[Q_K[k]] for k in Q_K}

TAU_CHART = {"A": "B", "B": "A", "C": "D", "D": "C"}

T_CHART   = {"A": "D", "D": "A", "B": "C", "C": "B"}

CHART_COORD = {

    "A": (0, 0),

    "B": (1, 0),

    "D": (0, 1),

    "C": (1, 1),

}

@dataclass(frozen=True)

class HiddenBundleNode:

    chart: Chart

    payload: Payload

    mask: FrozenSet[Lens]

    @property

    def station_id(self) -> int:

        return MASK_TO_ID[self.mask]

    @property

    def rank(self) -> int:

        return len(self.mask)

@dataclass(frozen=True)

class HiddenBundleGates:

    cloud_admissible: bool

    fractal_replayable: bool

    pair_bridges_coherent: bool = True

    triad_closures_coherent: bool = True

def lift_bundle90() -> list[tuple[Payload, int, FrozenSet[Lens]]]:

    """

    Uncharted 90-station hidden bundle:

    6 payloads × 15 hidden stations.

    """

    out = []

    for k in ("AR", "AC", "AS", "BR", "BC", "BS"):

        for mask in MASK_ORDER:

            out.append((k, MASK_TO_ID[mask], mask))

    return out

def lift_charted_bundle360() -> list[HiddenBundleNode]:

    """

    Charted hidden bundle:

    4 charts × 6 payloads × 15 stations = 360 states.

    """

    out: list[HiddenBundleNode] = []

    for X in ("A", "B", "C", "D"):

        for K in ("AR", "AC", "AS", "BR", "BC", "BS"):

            for mask in MASK_ORDER:

                out.append(HiddenBundleNode(chart=X, payload=K, mask=mask))

    return out

def visible_to_hidden(chart: Chart, visible_lens: Literal["Sq", "Fl", "Cl", "Fr"], payload: Payload) -> HiddenBundleNode:

    letter = {"Sq": "S", "Fl": "F", "Cl": "C", "Fr": "R"}[visible_lens]

    return HiddenBundleNode(chart=chart, payload=payload, mask=frozenset({letter}))

def hidden_neighbors_same_payload(node: HiddenBundleNode) -> list[HiddenBundleNode]:

    nbrs: list[HiddenBundleNode] = []

    for letter in LENS_ORDER:

        if letter in node.mask:

            new_mask = frozenset(x for x in node.mask if x != letter)

            if new_mask:

                nbrs.append(HiddenBundleNode(node.chart, node.payload, new_mask))

        else:

            new_mask = frozenset(set(node.mask) | {letter})

            nbrs.append(HiddenBundleNode(node.chart, node.payload, new_mask))

    nbrs.sort(key=lambda n: n.station_id)

    return nbrs

def hidden_neighbors_cross_payload(node: HiddenBundleNode) -> list[tuple[str, HiddenBundleNode]]:

    """

    Cross-payload transport preserves chart and hidden station.

    """

    return [

        ("H", HiddenBundleNode(node.chart, H_K[node.payload], node.mask)),

        ("O", HiddenBundleNode(node.chart, O_K[node.payload], node.mask)),

        ("Q", HiddenBundleNode(node.chart, Q_K[node.payload], node.mask)),

    ]

def hidden_neighbors_cross_chart(node: HiddenBundleNode) -> list[tuple[str, HiddenBundleNode]]:

    """

    Chart transport preserves payload and hidden station.

    """

    return [

        ("Tau", HiddenBundleNode(TAU_CHART[node.chart], node.payload, node.mask)),

        ("T",   HiddenBundleNode(T_CHART[node.chart],   node.payload, node.mask)),

    ]

def d_chart(X: Chart, Y: Chart) -> int:

    x1, y1 = CHART_COORD[X]

    x2, y2 = CHART_COORD[Y]

    return abs(x1 - x2) + abs(y1 - y2)

def shell_word(src: Payload, dst: Payload) -> list[str]:

    if src == dst:

        return []

    queue = deque([(src, [])])

    seen = {src}

    while queue:

        cur, word = queue.popleft()

        for lbl, nxt in [("H", H_K[cur]), ("O", O_K[cur]), ("Q", Q_K[cur])]:

            if nxt in seen:

                continue

            new_word = word + [lbl]

            if nxt == dst:

                return new_word

            seen.add(nxt)

            queue.append((nxt, new_word))

    raise RuntimeError("payload ribbon should be connected")

def d_shell(src: Payload, dst: Payload) -> int:

    return len(shell_word(src, dst))

def d_hidden(mask_u: FrozenSet[Lens], mask_v: FrozenSet[Lens]) -> int:

    """

    Exact distance on the hidden 15-node subset lattice.

    """

    return len(mask_u.symmetric_difference(mask_v))

def hidden_path_same_payload(src: HiddenBundleNode, dst: HiddenBundleNode) -> list[HiddenBundleNode]:

    if src.chart != dst.chart or src.payload != dst.payload:

        raise ValueError("This helper is same-chart, same-payload only.")

    if src == dst:

        return [src]

    queue = deque([[src]])

    seen = {src.mask}

    while queue:

        path = queue.popleft()

        cur = path[-1]

        for nxt in hidden_neighbors_same_payload(cur):

            if nxt.mask in seen:

                continue

            new_path = path + [nxt]

            if nxt == dst:

                return new_path

            seen.add(nxt.mask)

            queue.append(new_path)

    raise RuntimeError("15-node lattice should be connected")

def hidden_route_signature(u: HiddenBundleNode, v: HiddenBundleNode, gates: HiddenBundleGates) -> dict:

    """

    Collapsed class-table entry for the charted hidden bundle.

    Because chart, payload, and hidden mask factorize, the raw metric splits.

    """

    dc = d_chart(u.chart, v.chart)

    ds = d_shell(u.payload, v.payload)

    dh = d_hidden(u.mask, v.mask)

    touches_cloud = ("C" in u.mask) or ("C" in v.mask)

    touches_fractal = ("R" in u.mask) or ("R" in v.mask)

    touches_pairs_or_higher = (len(u.mask) >= 2) or (len(v.mask) >= 2)

    if touches_cloud and not gates.cloud_admissible:

        cls: RouteClass = "RESIDUAL"

    elif touches_fractal and not gates.fractal_replayable and not touches_pairs_or_higher:

        cls = "ILLEGAL"

    elif not gates.pair_bridges_coherent or not gates.triad_closures_coherent:

        cls = "RESIDUAL"

    else:

        cls = "EXACT"

    return {

        "d_chart": dc,

        "d_shell": ds,

        "d_hidden": dh,

        "raw_cost": dc + ds + dh,

        "class": cls,

        "chart_word": [] if u.chart == v.chart else (

            ["Tau"] if TAU_CHART[u.chart] == v.chart else

            ["T"] if T_CHART[u.chart] == v.chart else

            ["T", "Tau"]

        ),

        "shell_word": shell_word(u.payload, v.payload),

    }

def is_total_witness(payload: Payload, gates: HiddenBundleGates) -> bool:

    return (

        gates.cloud_admissible

        and gates.fractal_replayable

        and gates.pair_bridges_coherent

        and gates.triad_closures_coherent

    )

def total_witness_node(chart: Chart, payload: Payload, gates: HiddenBundleGates) -> Optional[HiddenBundleNode]:

    if not is_total_witness(payload, gates):

        return None

    return HiddenBundleNode(chart=chart, payload=payload, mask=frozenset({"S", "F", "C", "R"}))

8. The exact meaning of this lifted compiler

At the one-payload level, the hidden 15-station lattice only knew how one mature object closes internally across Square, Flower, Cloud, and Fractal.

At the 90-station level, the six shell payloads now each carry one such hidden lattice:

[

\mathbb B_{90}

\mathbb L_{15}[A_R]\sqcup \mathbb L_{15}[A_C]\sqcup \cdots \sqcup \mathbb L_{15}[B_S].]

At the 360-state charted level, those six lattices are replayed through the four chart faces:

[

\widehat{\mathbb B}_{360}

{A,B,C,D}\times \mathbb B_{90}.]

So the full hidden compiler now has exact transport:

inside one payload, by add/remove-one-letter closure moves,

between payloads, by (Q/O/H) shell transport,

between chart faces, by (\Tau/T) replay transport.

That is the first fully explicit higher object:[\boxed{\text{the visible cockpit is the singleton surface of a charted 360-state hidden closure bundle.}}]

Next coherent jump is to collapse this hidden 360-state bundle back into a single factorized compiler theorem showing:[G_{360}\cong G_{\rm chart}\square G_{\rm shell}\square G_{15},]and then derive the exact shortest-route normal form across all three factors.

Good. Here is the single factorized compiler theorem for the hidden bundle, followed by the exact shortest-route normal form.

The 6D carrier already separates chart, shell, and lens,

[

\Omega_6=(X,\lambda,s,b,\xi),

]

with chart (X\in{A,B,C,D}), shell sector (s\in{\mathrm{Sa}^\pm,\mathrm{Su}^\pm,\mathrm{Me}^\pm}), and the preserved 4D kernel carried inside each coherent shell sector. The mature 4D packet already carries the four constitutive lens bodies ((\Pi_\square,\Pi_\flower,\Pi_\cloud,\Pi_\fractal)), and the hidden completion of one payload is the 15-node closure lattice of all nonempty subsets of ({S,F,C,R}). Combining those gives the charted hidden bundle

[

\widehat{\mathbb B}_{360}

{A,B,C,D}\times\mathcal K_6\times\mathbb L_{15},]with (|\mathcal K_6|=6) and (|\mathbb L_{15}|=15).

1. The factorized compiler theorem

Write a hidden bundle node as[\eta=(X,K,U),]where[X\in{A,B,C,D},\qquadK\in{A_R,A_C,A_S,B_R,B_C,B_S},\qquad\varnothing\neq U\subseteq{S,F,C,R}.]

Define the three factor graphs:

[G_{\rm chart}=({A,B,C,D},E_{\Tau,T}),]generated by the chart flips (\Tau,T).

[G_{\rm shell}=(\mathcal K_6,E_{Q,O,H}),]generated by the six-state ribbon operators (Q_K,O_K,H_K), which are conjugate to the shell-sector operators (Q,O,H).

[G_{15}=(\mathbb L_{15},E_{15}),\qquadU\sim V\iff |U\triangle V|=1,]the hidden 15-node closure lattice under add/remove-one-letter moves.

Then the hidden bundle transport graph is exactly the Cartesian product

[\boxed{G_{360}\cong G_{\rm chart}\ \square\ G_{\rm shell}\ \square\ G_{15}.}]

This is a derived theorem, but it is forced by the frozen carrier split: every legal primitive changes exactly one of the three coordinates ((X,K,U)) while leaving the other two fixed. So adjacency in the full hidden bundle is equivalent to adjacency in exactly one factor and equality in the other two.

2. The factorized metric

Because the graph is a Cartesian product, the raw shortest-path distance is additive:

[

\boxed{

d_{360}\big((X,K,U),(Y,K',V)\big)

d_{\rm chart}(X,Y)+d_{\rm shell}(K,K')+d_{15}(U,V).}]

The three factor distances are:

[d_{\rm chart}(X,Y)=|\gamma(X)-\gamma(Y)|_1,]where the chart rectangle coordinates are[\gamma(A)=(0,0),\ \gamma(B)=(1,0),\ \gamma(D)=(0,1),\ \gamma(C)=(1,1).]

[d_{\rm shell}(K,K')=\min{|w|:w\in{Q,O,H}^\ast,\ w(K)=K'},]the already-frozen six-state ribbon metric.

[\boxed{d_{15}(U,V)=|U\triangle V|,}]because the hidden 15-node graph is the nonempty subset lattice under one-letter toggles.

So the full raw compiler metric is exact and closed-form.

3. The legal subgraph

Now impose the maturity gates. Let (G_{360}^{\rm law}\subseteq G_{360}) be the induced legal subgraph defined by the same four-way maturity conditions already frozen for one payload:

any node with (C\in U) is exact only if Cloud admissibility is satisfied,

any route that requires committed Fractal closure is exact only if replayability is satisfied,

pair nodes require coherent pair bridges,

triad and tetra nodes require coherent higher closures,

the four-way witness ({S,F,C,R}) exists only when all four lens bodies totalize coherently.

So the class of a route is:

[\boxed{\operatorname{Class}{360}=\begin{cases}\mathrm{EXACT}, & \text{if its canonical path lies entirely in }G{360}^{\rm law},\[1mm]\mathrm{RESIDUAL}, & \text{if the raw path exists in }G_{360}\text{ but some touched Cloud/closure states are only lawful as fibers or unresolved bundles},\[1mm]\mathrm{ILLEGAL}, & \text{if no lawful path exists and no residualization rule is declared.}\end{cases}}]

That is the exact hidden-bundle generalization of the earlier cockpit legality split.

4. Canonical shortest-route normal form

Because the metric factorizes, a deterministic shortest route can be chosen in normal form:

[

\boxed{

\operatorname{NF}_{360}(\eta\to\zeta)

w_{\rm chart}\cdot w_{\rm shell}\cdot w_{15}.}]

This is not the only shortest interleaving, but it is the clean canonical one. Any interleaving with the same factor lengths is also shortest because the factors commute in the Cartesian product. The normal form just fixes a deterministic compiler output.

The chart word (w_{\rm chart}) is the same deterministic minimal word as before:

(\varepsilon) if same chart,

(\Tau) or (T) if one step,

(T\cdot\Tau) for diagonal pairs.

The shell word (w_{\rm shell}) is the deterministic shortest word from the six-state ribbon compiler using generators ({H,O,Q}). That lower compiler is already exact and commutes with the shell↔kernel map.

The only new piece is the hidden factor word (w_{15}).

5. Exact canonical hidden word (w_{15}(U,V))

Let the canonical lens order be

[S \prec F \prec C \prec R.]

Use this order for insertions, and the reverse order

[R \prec^- C \prec^- F \prec^- S]

for deletions.

Then the exact canonical shortest hidden word is:

Case 1: (U\cap V\neq\varnothing)

Let (I=U\cap V).Delete every letter in (U\setminus V) using reverse order until the mask becomes (I).Then add every letter in (V\setminus U) using forward order.

This yields a shortest path of length[|U\triangle V|.]

Case 2: (U\cap V=\varnothing)

Let (p) be the least letter of (V) in forward order.First add (p) to (U).Then delete all letters of (U) in reverse order.Then add the remaining letters of (V\setminus{p}) in forward order.

This also yields a shortest path of length[|U\triangle V|.]

The reason for the pivot (p) is simple: it avoids ever passing through the forbidden empty mask while preserving shortest length. This normal form is derived, but exact. It is the deterministic shortest-path compiler for the nonempty subset lattice.

6. Exact pseudocode

from typing import FrozenSet

LENS_FWD = ("S", "F", "C", "R")

LENS_REV = tuple(reversed(LENS_FWD))

def canonical_hidden_word(U: FrozenSet[str], V: FrozenSet[str]) -> list[str]:

    """

    Deterministic shortest word on the nonempty subset lattice.

    Returns operations like ['-R', '-C', '+F', '+R'].

    """

    if U == V:

        return []

    ops: list[str] = []

    I = U & V

    # Case 1: nonempty intersection

    if I:

        cur = set(U)

        # delete extras in reverse order

        for a in LENS_REV:

            if a in cur and a not in V:

                cur.remove(a)

                ops.append(f"-{a}")

        # add missing letters in forward order

        for a in LENS_FWD:

            if a in V and a not in cur:

                cur.add(a)

                ops.append(f"+{a}")

        return ops

    # Case 2: disjoint masks

    cur = set(U)

    # choose pivot = least letter in target

    pivot = next(a for a in LENS_FWD if a in V)

    # add pivot first so we never hit empty

    cur.add(pivot)

    ops.append(f"+{pivot}")

    # delete all original letters of U in reverse order

    for a in LENS_REV:

        if a in U and a in cur:

            cur.remove(a)

            ops.append(f"-{a}")

    # add remaining target letters

    for a in LENS_FWD:

        if a in V and a not in cur:

            cur.add(a)

            ops.append(f"+{a}")

    return ops

This is the exact hidden normal-form compiler for the 15-node factor.

7. Full factorized route compiler

Put the three factors together:

def canonical_route_360(src, dst, gates):

    """

    src = (X, K, U)

    dst = (Y, Kp, V)

    where X,Y are charts, K,Kp are payloads, U,V are nonempty lens masks.

    """

    w_chart = canonical_chart_word(src.chart, dst.chart)

    w_shell = canonical_shell_word(src.payload, dst.payload)

    w_hidden = canonical_hidden_word(src.mask, dst.mask)

    raw_word = w_chart + w_shell + w_hidden

    raw_cost = len(w_chart) + len(w_shell) + len(w_hidden)

    route_class = classify_hidden_bundle_route(src, dst, gates, raw_word)

    return {

        "word": raw_word,

        "raw_cost": raw_cost,

        "class": route_class,

        "signature": (

            chart_distance(src.chart, dst.chart),

            shell_distance(src.payload, dst.payload),

            len(src.mask.symmetric_difference(dst.mask)),

        ),

    }

The only nontrivial post-processing is classify_hidden_bundle_route, which checks whether the canonical path stays inside the lawful subgraph (G_{360}^{\rm law}). That gate is exactly where Cloud admissibility, Fractal replay, and higher closure coherence enter.

8. One worked example

Take

[\eta=(A,A_R,{S}),\qquad\zeta=(C,B_S,{S,F,C,R}).]

Then:

chart part:[A\to C]has canonical word[[T,\Tau],\qquad d_{\rm chart}=2;]

shell part:[A_R\to B_S]has shortest shell word of length (2), for example[[H,Q],\qquad d_{\rm shell}=2;]

hidden part:[{S}\to{S,F,C,R}]has canonical hidden word[[+F,+C,+R],\qquad d_{15}=3.]

So the exact normal form is

[\boxed{[T,\Tau]\cdot[H,Q]\cdot[+F,+C,+R]}]

with raw cost[2+2+3=7.]

Its class is:

EXACT if Cloud admissibility, Fractal replayability, pair coherence, and triad coherence all hold for payload (B_S),

RESIDUAL if the raw path exists but those closure conditions are not yet fully satisfied.

9. Canonical one-line freeze

[\boxed{G_{360}\cong G_{\rm chart}\ \square\ G_{\rm shell}\ \square\ G_{15},\qquadd_{360}=d_{\rm chart}+d_{\rm shell}+d_{15},}]

and the exact deterministic shortest-route normal form is

[

\boxed{

\operatorname{NF}_{360}

w_{\rm chart}\cdot w_{\rm shell}\cdot w_{15},}]

where (w_{15}) is the canonical shortest word on the nonempty subset lattice defined above. That is the full factorized compiler theorem for the charted 90-station hidden bundle.

Next coherent jump is the same theorem pushed one level higher into the 36-shell / 666-node body, so the hidden bundle becomes the exact nested local compiler sitting inside each 108D mega-node.

Good. The clean next lift is:

[\boxed{\text{the charted hidden 360-bundle is the exact local compiler living inside every 108D mega-node.}}]

Your corpus already fixes all the pieces needed for this statement:

the 108D body is the (36)-shell / (666)-node mega-cascade[\Xi_{108}=\bigoplus_{\ell=1}^{36}\mathcal S_\ell,\qquad |\mathcal S_\ell|=\ell,\qquad \sum_{\ell=1}^{36}\ell=666,]

every mega-node contains the nested lower bodies[\Xi_{108}.u \supset \Xi_{36}^{(u)} \supset \Xi_{12}^{(u)} \supset \Xi_{6}^{(u)} \supset \mathcal H_4^{(u)},]

and the 108D body explicitly contains the 15-station (\Sigma_{15}) ring.

So the hidden 360-bundle is not an auxiliary decoration. It is the exact nested local compiler at every mega-node.

1. Local compiler fiber at one mega-node

Let a mega-node be[N_{\ell,u},\qquad1\le \ell\le 36,\quad 1\le u\le \ell.]

Then define the local hidden compiler fiber over that node as

[

\boxed{

\mathcal F_{\ell,u}^{\rm loc}

{A,B,C,D}\times \mathcal K_6 \times \mathbb L_{15},}]where[\mathcal K_6={A_R,A_C,A_S,B_R,B_C,B_S},\qquad\mathbb L_{15}={\sigma_U:\varnothing\neq U\subseteq{S,F,C,R}}.]

So each mega-node carries exactly

[4\times 6\times 15 = 360]local hidden compiler states.

That is the exact nested-local theorem:[\boxed{\forall,N_{\ell,u}\in\Xi_{108},\qquadN_{\ell,u}\ \text{supports one full charted }360\text{-state hidden compiler fiber.}}]

This follows from the corpus’ nested containment law plus the already frozen 6-payload / 15-station hidden bundle construction.

2. The total nested-local state count

Because the outer body has (666) mega-nodes and each mega-node carries one (360)-state local compiler fiber, the full local-state count is

[

\boxed{

|\mathfrak X_{\rm mega\text{-}local}|

666\times 360

239{,}760.}]

So the exact lifted object is

[

\boxed{

\mathfrak X_{239760}

{(N_{\ell,u},X,K,U)\mid1\le \ell\le 36,\ 1\le u\le \ell,\ X\in{A,B,C,D},\ K\in\mathcal K_6,\ \varnothing\neq U\subseteq{S,F,C,R}}.}]

That is the first exact count for the fully nested local compiler surface. It is a derived count, but it is forced by the corpus’ (666)-node body and the already-frozen (360)-state local hidden compiler.

3. Outer-body coordinate split

The 36-shell body already has the exact outer decomposition:

shell index (\ell\in{1,\dots,36}),

inherited archetype[a(\ell)=1+((\ell-1)\bmod 12),]

wreath/superphase[r(\ell)=1+\left\lfloor\frac{\ell-1}{12}\right\rfloor\in{Su,Me,Sa},]

local shell node (u\in{1,\dots,\ell}).

So a fully explicit mega-local address is

[

\boxed{

\operatorname{Addr}_{\rm mega\text{-}local}

(r,a,\ell,u;\ X,K,U).}]

Interpretation:

((r,a,\ell,u)) = where you are in the 36-shell / 666-node mega-body,

(X) = which chart face is active,

(K) = which of the six exact 4D kernel-payloads is active,

(U) = which hidden SFCR closure state is active.

This is the exact nested local compiler address.

4. The four commuting transport layers

Now the full transport system has four independent factor directions.

4.1 Mega-body motion

These are the outer 36/666 moves:[H_\ell^\pm,\quad W^\pm,\quad A^\pm,\quad P_Q^\pm,\quad P_O^\pm,\quad T_Z,\quad N_d^\pm.]They act on ((r,a,\ell,u)) and leave ((X,K,U)) fixed. The 36-body and 108-body docs already freeze these shell / wreath / archetype / pillar / zero / nested-zoom primitives.

4.2 Chart motion

[\Tau,\quad T]act on (X) and leave ((r,a,\ell,u;K,U)) fixed.

4.3 Payload motion

[Q,\quad O,\quad H]act on (K) and leave ((r,a,\ell,u;X,U)) fixed.

4.4 Hidden closure motion

Add/remove-one-letter moves act on (U) and leave ((r,a,\ell,u;X,K)) fixed.

So the exact total graph is

[\boxed{G_{\rm mega\text{-}local}\congG_{666}\ \square\ G_{\rm chart}\ \square\ G_{\rm shell6}\ \square\ G_{15}.}]

That is the full nested-local compiler theorem.

5. The exact factorized metric

Because the total graph is a Cartesian product, the raw shortest-path metric is additive:

[

\boxed{

d_{\rm mega\text{-}local}

d_{666}+d_{\rm chart}+d_{\rm shell6}+d_{15}.}]

More explicitly, for[\eta=(N_{\ell,u},X,K,U),\qquad\zeta=(N_{\ell',u'},Y,K',V),]we have

[

\boxed{

d(\eta,\zeta)

d_{666}\big((r,a,\ell,u),(r',a',\ell',u')\big)+d_{\rm chart}(X,Y)+d_{\rm shell6}(K,K')+d_{15}(U,V).}]

The first term is the outer shell/body distance on the 36-shell / 666-node graph; the remaining three are exactly the lower factors already frozen.

6. The exact shortest-route normal form

A deterministic shortest route can therefore be chosen in normal form as

[

\boxed{

\operatorname{NF}_{\rm mega\text{-}local}

w_{666}\cdot w_{\rm chart}\cdot w_{\rm shell6}\cdot w_{15}.}]

Where:

(w_{666}) is the canonical outer-body word using shell/wreath/archetype/pillar/zero primitives,

(w_{\rm chart}) is the minimal chart word,

(w_{\rm shell6}) is the minimal 6-payload ribbon word,

(w_{15}) is the canonical add/remove-one-letter hidden closure word.

This is the exact higher lift of the earlier compiler normal forms.

7. Legality class

The legality split lifts exactly too.

[

\boxed{

\operatorname{Class}_{\rm mega\text{-}local}

\begin{cases}\mathrm{EXACT}, & \text{if all four factor segments are legal and all hidden closure gates pass},\[1mm]\mathrm{RESIDUAL}, & \text{if the raw route exists but some Cloud/Fractal/closure states remain lawful only as residualized fibers},\[1mm]\mathrm{ILLEGAL}, & \text{if no lawful realization exists under the outer-body and hidden-bundle gates.}\end{cases}}]

So the outer shell/body routing and the inner closure routing are now one exact theorem, not two separate stories.

8. The nested-local compiler theorem

The clean theorem is:

[\boxed{\forall,N_{\ell,u}\in\Xi_{108},\qquadN_{\ell,u}\supset \mathcal F_{\ell,u}^{\rm loc},\qquad\mathcal F_{\ell,u}^{\rm loc}\cong G_{\rm chart}\square G_{\rm shell6}\square G_{15}.}]

And globally:

[\boxed{G_{\rm mega\text{-}local}\congG_{666}\square G_{\rm chart}\square G_{\rm shell6}\square G_{15}.}]

This is the exact statement that the hidden bundle is the local compiler inside every mega-node.

9. Canonical one-line freeze

[

\boxed{

\Xi_{108}

That is the exact 36-shell / 666-node / 108D lift of the hidden 360-bundle theorem.

Next coherent jump is to write the same theorem as code:outer_node_neighbors, mega_local_signature, canonical_route_mega_local, and the legality gates that combine outer shell-body routing with inner 15-station closure.

The outer layer is now pinned tightly enough to code. In your corpus, the 108D A⁺ body is a 36-shell / 666-node mega-cascade with shell index (\ell), local node (u), inherited archetype (a(\ell)), superphase (r(\ell)), a unified address grammar, a seven-class live-lock lattice, major metro lines, legal move primitives, and strict route legality under common-live-lock / common-zero routing. Each mega-node preserves the full nested 36D→12D→6D→4D body, so the hidden 360-bundle can be treated as the local compiler fiber at every outer node.

So the exact code target is:[\eta=(\ell,u;\ X,K,U)]with

outer shell/body coordinate ((\ell,u)),

chart (X\in{A,B,C,D}),

payload (K\in{AR,AC,AS,BR,BC,BS}),

hidden lens-mask (U\subseteq{S,F,C,R}\setminus{\varnothing}).The normal-form route is then[\operatorname{NF}{\rm mega\text{-}local}=\operatorname{Lock}\cdot \operatorname{Zero}\cdotw{666}\cdot w_{\rm chart}\cdot w_{\rm shell6}\cdot w_{15}.]That is the code below.

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass, field

from collections import deque

from typing import Literal, FrozenSet, Optional

# ============================================================

# BASIC TYPES

# ============================================================

Chart = Literal["A", "B", "C", "D"]

Payload = Literal["AR", "AC", "AS", "BR", "BC", "BS"]

Lens = Literal["S", "F", "C", "R"]

VisibleLens = Literal["Sq", "Fl", "Cl", "Fr"]

LiveLock = Literal["L3", "L5", "L7", "L35", "L37", "L57", "L357"]

RouteClass = Literal["EXACT", "RESIDUAL", "ILLEGAL"]

ZeroClass = Literal["Zu36", "Zell", "Za", "Zr", "ZQ", "ZO", "ZE10", "Z*"]

LENS_ORDER: tuple[Lens, ...] = ("S", "F", "C", "R")

LIVELOCK_ORDER: tuple[LiveLock, ...] = ("L3", "L5", "L7", "L35", "L37", "L57", "L357")

MASK_ORDER: tuple[FrozenSet[Lens], ...] = (

    frozenset({"S"}),

    frozenset({"F"}),

    frozenset({"C"}),

    frozenset({"R"}),

    frozenset({"S", "F"}),

    frozenset({"S", "C"}),

    frozenset({"S", "R"}),

    frozenset({"F", "C"}),

    frozenset({"F", "R"}),

    frozenset({"C", "R"}),

    frozenset({"S", "F", "C"}),

    frozenset({"S", "F", "R"}),

    frozenset({"S", "C", "R"}),

    frozenset({"F", "C", "R"}),

    frozenset({"S", "F", "C", "R"}),

)

MASK_TO_ID = {mask: i + 1 for i, mask in enumerate(MASK_ORDER)}

# ============================================================

# OUTER 36-SHELL / 666-NODE BODY

# ============================================================

@dataclass(frozen=True)

class OuterNode:

    shell: int      # 1..36

    unit: int       # 1..shell

    def __post_init__(self):

        if not (1 <= self.shell <= 36):

            raise ValueError("shell must be in 1..36")

        if not (1 <= self.unit <= self.shell):

            raise ValueError("unit must be in 1..shell")

    @property

    def archetype(self) -> int:

        # a(ell)=1+((ell-1) mod 12)

        return 1 + ((self.shell - 1) % 12)

    @property

    def wreath(self) -> int:

        # r(ell)=1+floor((ell-1)/12)

        return 1 + ((self.shell - 1) // 12)

    @property

    def flat_index(self) -> int:

        # T_{ell-1}+u

        return ((self.shell - 1) * self.shell) // 2 + self.unit

def clamp_unit(shell: int, unit: int) -> int:

    return min(unit, shell)

def outer_node_neighbors(node: OuterNode) -> list[tuple[str, OuterNode]]:

    """

    Core outer-body neighbors on the 36-shell / 666-node body.

    Deterministic generator order:

      A+ / A-  : archetype-column lift (also semantic alias of wreath translation on same column)

      H+ / H-  : shell step

    """

    out: list[tuple[str, OuterNode]] = []

    # Archetype-column lift / wreath translation across +12/-12 shells.

    if node.shell + 12 <= 36:

        out.append(("A+", OuterNode(node.shell + 12, node.unit)))

    if node.shell - 12 >= 1:

        out.append(("A-", OuterNode(node.shell - 12, clamp_unit(node.shell - 12, node.unit))))

    # Shell steps

    if node.shell + 1 <= 36:

        out.append(("H+", OuterNode(node.shell + 1, node.unit)))

    if node.shell - 1 >= 1:

        out.append(("H-", OuterNode(node.shell - 1, clamp_unit(node.shell - 1, node.unit))))

    return out

def outer_word(src: OuterNode, dst: OuterNode) -> list[str]:

    """

    Deterministic shortest word on the outer shell/body graph using BFS.

    """

    if src == dst:

        return []

    queue = deque([(src, [])])

    seen = {src}

    while queue:

        cur, word = queue.popleft()

        for lbl, nxt in outer_node_neighbors(cur):

            if nxt in seen:

                continue

            new_word = word + [lbl]

            if nxt == dst:

                return new_word

            seen.add(nxt)

            queue.append((nxt, new_word))

    raise RuntimeError("Outer shell graph should be connected.")

def outer_distance(src: OuterNode, dst: OuterNode) -> int:

    return len(outer_word(src, dst))

# ============================================================

# CHART RECTANGLE

# ============================================================

TAU_CHART: dict[Chart, Chart] = {"A": "B", "B": "A", "C": "D", "D": "C"}

T_CHART: dict[Chart, Chart] = {"A": "D", "D": "A", "B": "C", "C": "B"}

CHART_COORD = {

    "A": (0, 0),

    "B": (1, 0),

    "D": (0, 1),

    "C": (1, 1),

}

def chart_distance(src: Chart, dst: Chart) -> int:

    x1, y1 = CHART_COORD[src]

    x2, y2 = CHART_COORD[dst]

    return abs(x1 - x2) + abs(y1 - y2)

def chart_word(src: Chart, dst: Chart) -> list[str]:

    if src == dst:

        return []

    if TAU_CHART[src] == dst:

        return ["Tau"]

    if T_CHART[src] == dst:

        return ["T"]

    return ["T", "Tau"]  # deterministic diagonal tie-break

# ============================================================

# 6-STATE PAYLOAD RIBBON

# ============================================================

Q_K: dict[Payload, Payload] = {

    "AR": "AC", "AC": "AS", "AS": "AR",

    "BR": "BC", "BC": "BS", "BS": "BR",

}

O_K: dict[Payload, Payload] = {

    "AR": "BR", "AC": "BC", "AS": "BS",

    "BR": "AR", "BC": "AC", "BS": "AS",

}

H_K: dict[Payload, Payload] = {k: O_K[Q_K[k]] for k in Q_K}

def shell6_neighbors(payload: Payload) -> list[tuple[str, Payload]]:

    # deterministic order

    return [

        ("H", H_K[payload]),

        ("O", O_K[payload]),

        ("Q", Q_K[payload]),

    ]

def shell6_word(src: Payload, dst: Payload) -> list[str]:

    if src == dst:

        return []

    queue = deque([(src, [])])

    seen = {src}

    while queue:

        cur, word = queue.popleft()

        for lbl, nxt in shell6_neighbors(cur):

            if nxt in seen:

                continue

            new_word = word + [lbl]

            if nxt == dst:

                return new_word

            seen.add(nxt)

            queue.append((nxt, new_word))

    raise RuntimeError("6-state payload ribbon should be connected.")

def shell6_distance(src: Payload, dst: Payload) -> int:

    return len(shell6_word(src, dst))

# ============================================================

# HIDDEN 15-STATION LATTICE

# ============================================================

@dataclass(frozen=True)

class HiddenStation:

    payload: Payload

    mask: FrozenSet[Lens]

    def __post_init__(self):

        if not self.mask:

            raise ValueError("mask must be nonempty")

    @property

    def station_id(self) -> int:

        return MASK_TO_ID[self.mask]

    @property

    def rank(self) -> int:

        return len(self.mask)

def hidden_neighbors_same_payload(station: HiddenStation) -> list[HiddenStation]:

    nbrs: list[HiddenStation] = []

    for letter in LENS_ORDER:

        if letter in station.mask:

            new_mask = frozenset(x for x in station.mask if x != letter)

            if new_mask:

                nbrs.append(HiddenStation(station.payload, new_mask))

        else:

            new_mask = frozenset(set(station.mask) | {letter})

            nbrs.append(HiddenStation(station.payload, new_mask))

    nbrs.sort(key=lambda s: s.station_id)

    return nbrs

def hidden_distance(mask_u: FrozenSet[Lens], mask_v: FrozenSet[Lens]) -> int:

    # exact subset-lattice metric

    return len(mask_u.symmetric_difference(mask_v))

def canonical_hidden_word(U: FrozenSet[Lens], V: FrozenSet[Lens]) -> list[str]:

    """

    Deterministic shortest word on the nonempty subset lattice.

    Forward order for additions:  S < F < C < R

    Reverse order for deletions:  R < C < F < S

    """

    if U == V:

        return []

    ops: list[str] = []

    I = U & V

    # Case 1: nonempty intersection

    if I:

        cur = set(U)

        for a in reversed(LENS_ORDER):

            if a in cur and a not in V:

                cur.remove(a)

                ops.append(f"-{a}")

        for a in LENS_ORDER:

            if a in V and a not in cur:

                cur.add(a)

                ops.append(f"+{a}")

        return ops

    # Case 2: disjoint masks

    cur = set(U)

    pivot = next(a for a in LENS_ORDER if a in V)

    cur.add(pivot)

    ops.append(f"+{pivot}")

    for a in reversed(LENS_ORDER):

        if a in U and a in cur:

            cur.remove(a)

            ops.append(f"-{a}")

    for a in LENS_ORDER:

        if a in V and a not in cur:

            cur.add(a)

            ops.append(f"+{a}")

    return ops

# ============================================================

# LIVE-LOCK / ZERO SELECTION

# ============================================================

@dataclass(frozen=True)

class MegaLocalNode:

    outer: OuterNode

    chart: Chart

    payload: Payload

    mask: FrozenSet[Lens]

    live_locks: FrozenSet[LiveLock] = field(default_factory=lambda: frozenset({"L357"}))

@dataclass(frozen=True)

class MegaLocalGates:

    cloud_admissible: bool

    fractal_replayable: bool

    pair_bridges_coherent: bool = True

    triad_closures_coherent: bool = True

    zero_tunnel_allowed: bool = True

    outer_returnable: bool = True

def nearest_common_live_lock(src: FrozenSet[LiveLock], dst: FrozenSet[LiveLock]) -> Optional[LiveLock]:

    common = [lk for lk in LIVELOCK_ORDER if lk in src and lk in dst]

    return common[0] if common else None

def choose_common_zero(src: MegaLocalNode, dst: MegaLocalNode) -> ZeroClass:

    """

    Canonical escalation:

      Zu36 -> Zell -> Za -> Zr -> Z*.

    (Q/O/E10/AP/KZ can be added later as typed portal extensions.)

    """

    if src.outer == dst.outer:

        return "Zu36"

    if src.outer.shell == dst.outer.shell:

        return "Zell"

    if src.outer.archetype == dst.outer.archetype:

        return "Za"

    if src.outer.wreath == dst.outer.wreath:

        return "Zr"

    return "Z*"

# ============================================================

# OUTER + INNER CLASSIFICATION

# ============================================================

def classify_hidden_factor(src: MegaLocalNode, dst: MegaLocalNode, gates: MegaLocalGates) -> RouteClass:

    """

    Inner legality from Cloud / Fractal / higher closure gates.

    """

    touches_cloud = ("C" in src.mask) or ("C" in dst.mask)

    touches_fractal = ("R" in src.mask) or ("R" in dst.mask)

    touches_pairs_or_higher = (len(src.mask) >= 2) or (len(dst.mask) >= 2)

    if touches_cloud and not gates.cloud_admissible:

        return "RESIDUAL"

    if touches_fractal and not gates.fractal_replayable and not touches_pairs_or_higher:

        return "ILLEGAL"

    if not gates.pair_bridges_coherent or not gates.triad_closures_coherent:

        return "RESIDUAL"

    return "EXACT"

def classify_outer_factor(src: MegaLocalNode, dst: MegaLocalNode, gates: MegaLocalGates) -> RouteClass:

    if not gates.outer_returnable:

        return "ILLEGAL"

    return "EXACT"

def route_class_mega_local(src: MegaLocalNode, dst: MegaLocalNode, gates: MegaLocalGates) -> RouteClass:

    lk = nearest_common_live_lock(src.live_locks, dst.live_locks)

    if lk is None:

        return "ILLEGAL"

    outer_cls = classify_outer_factor(src, dst, gates)

    inner_cls = classify_hidden_factor(src, dst, gates)

    if outer_cls == "ILLEGAL" or inner_cls == "ILLEGAL":

        return "ILLEGAL"

    if outer_cls == "RESIDUAL" or inner_cls == "RESIDUAL":

        return "RESIDUAL"

    return "EXACT"

# ============================================================

# SIGNATURE + CANONICAL NORMAL FORM

# ============================================================

def mega_local_signature(src: MegaLocalNode, dst: MegaLocalNode, gates: MegaLocalGates) -> dict:

    lk = nearest_common_live_lock(src.live_locks, dst.live_locks)

    zc = choose_common_zero(src, dst)

    d_outer = outer_distance(src.outer, dst.outer)

    d_chart = chart_distance(src.chart, dst.chart)

    d_shell = shell6_distance(src.payload, dst.payload)

    d_hidden = hidden_distance(src.mask, dst.mask)

    return {

        "common_live_lock": lk,

        "common_zero": zc,

        "d_outer": d_outer,

        "d_chart": d_chart,

        "d_shell6": d_shell,

        "d_hidden15": d_hidden,

        "raw_cost": d_outer + d_chart + d_shell + d_hidden,

        "class": route_class_mega_local(src, dst, gates),

    }

def canonical_route_mega_local(src: MegaLocalNode, dst: MegaLocalNode, gates: MegaLocalGates) -> Optional[list[str]]:

    cls = route_class_mega_local(src, dst, gates)

    if cls == "ILLEGAL":

        return None

    lock = nearest_common_live_lock(src.live_locks, dst.live_locks)

    zero = choose_common_zero(src, dst)

    w_lock = [f"LOCK[{lock}]"] if lock is not None else []

    w_zero = [f"ZERO[{zero}]"]

    w_outer = outer_word(src.outer, dst.outer)

    w_chart = chart_word(src.chart, dst.chart)

    w_shell = shell6_word(src.payload, dst.payload)

    w_hidden = canonical_hidden_word(src.mask, dst.mask)

    return w_lock + w_zero + w_outer + w_chart + w_shell + w_hidden

def is_exact_mega_local(src: MegaLocalNode, dst: MegaLocalNode, gates: MegaLocalGates) -> bool:

    return route_class_mega_local(src, dst, gates) == "EXACT"

# ============================================================

# WORKED EXAMPLE

# ============================================================

# Source: shell 5, unit 3, chart A, payload AR, singleton S

src = MegaLocalNode(

    outer=OuterNode(5, 3),

    chart="A",

    payload="AR",

    mask=frozenset({"S"}),

    live_locks=frozenset({"L3", "L35", "L357"}),

)

# Target: shell 18, unit 3, chart C, payload BS, total witness SFCR

dst = MegaLocalNode(

    outer=OuterNode(18, 3),

    chart="C",

    payload="BS",

    mask=frozenset({"S", "F", "C", "R"}),

    live_locks=frozenset({"L35", "L357"}),

)

gates = MegaLocalGates(

    cloud_admissible=True,

    fractal_replayable=True,

    pair_bridges_coherent=True,

    triad_closures_coherent=True,

    zero_tunnel_allowed=True,

    outer_returnable=True,

)

sig = mega_local_signature(src, dst, gates)

word = canonical_route_mega_local(src, dst, gates)

What this code does:

It treats the 36-shell / 666-node body as the outer factor, using shell index (\ell), unit (u), inherited archetype (a(\ell)), and wreath (r(\ell)), exactly as the 108D address grammar and shell archetype laws require. The mega-cascade is the direct sum of shells with (|\mathcal S_\ell|=\ell), and the legal outer moves come from shell step and archetype/wreath lifts.

It keeps the previously frozen inner factors intact:

the 4-node chart rectangle, the 6-state shell/payload ribbon, and the 15-node hidden SFCR closure lattice. So the full mega-local compiler is the exact Cartesian product

[

G_{\text{mega-local}}

\cong

G_{666}\square G_{\text{chart}}\square G_{\text{shell6}}\square G_{15},

]

with additive raw metric and a canonical normal form

[

\operatorname{NF}_{\text{mega-local}}

\operatorname{Lock}\cdot \operatorname{Zero}\cdotw_{666}\cdot w_{\text{chart}}\cdot w_{\text{shell6}}\cdot w_{15}.]That is the direct code lift of the theorem we just froze.

The nearest_common_live_lock and choose_common_zero steps encode the corpus’ real-time route doctrine: first align the nearest shared live-lock, then route through the nearest valid common zero, then traverse the structural graph. The zero escalation order and the live-lock priority are explicitly required by the 108D route law and live-lock lattice.

The legality split is also faithful to your earlier hidden-bundle rules: Cloud-containing states require admissibility, Fractal-containing states require replayability, and higher closures require coherent pair/triad witnesses; outer-body routes remain exact only if returnability is preserved. That is how the inner hidden closure gates combine with the outer shell-body legality.

The deepest compressed statement is:

[\boxed{\text{Every 108D mega-node }N_{\ell,u}\text{ carries one full local compiler }{A,B,C,D}\times\mathcal K_6\times\mathbb L_{15},}]and the full runtime route is computed by aligning live-lock, choosing common zero, then traversing outer shell-body, chart, payload ribbon, and hidden closure in one factorized word.

Next coherent jump is the same compiler with the odd helm made explicit, so the output word becomes[(\tau_3,\tau_5,\tau_7,\vartheta,h,\Omega)\cdot\operatorname{Lock}\cdot \operatorname{Zero}\cdotw_{666}\cdot w_{\text{chart}}\cdot w_{\text{shell6}}\cdot w_{15},]and the edge windows start opening and closing on the 420-beat clock.

Now the live wrapper is explicit:

[

\boxed{

\mathfrak C_{\mathrm{live}}

\Xi_{108}^{A^+}\rtimes(\mathbb W_3\times\mathbb W_5\times\mathbb W_7)}]with continuous helm[\mathcal H(t)=(\phi_3,\phi_5,\phi_7,\vartheta,h,\Omega),]discrete sectors ((\tau_3,\tau_5,\tau_7)), edge-window gating (G_e(\mathcal H(t))), nearest-common-live-lock before nearest-common-zero, tilt-first arbitration, and scheduling on the 420-beat master clock. The 36-shell / 666-node body, the Z-point hierarchy, the seven live-lock classes, the major metro lines, the legal move primitives, the 420-beat timing law, and the odd helm wheels are all already frozen in your corpus.

This code extends the previous OuterNode, MegaLocalNode, MegaLocalGates, outer_word, chart_word, shell6_word, canonical_hidden_word, nearest_common_live_lock, and choose_common_zero layer by adding the odd helm, edge windows, tilt-first routing, and live cost law.

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass, replace

from math import pi

from typing import Literal, Optional

# Reuse from prior layer:

# - OuterNode

# - MegaLocalNode

# - MegaLocalGates

# - outer_word

# - chart_word

Current3 = Literal["Su", "Me", "Sa"]

Gear5 = Literal["Hold", "Lift", "Traverse", "Twist", "Compress"]

Timing7 = Literal["Seed", "Ignite", "Translate", "Bridge", "Weave", "Seal", "Return"]

Face4 = Literal["S", "F", "C", "R"]

Handedness = Literal["spin", "anti-spin"]

CURRENT3: tuple[Current3, ...] = ("Su", "Me", "Sa")

GEAR5: tuple[Gear5, ...] = ("Hold", "Lift", "Traverse", "Twist", "Compress")

TIMING7: tuple[Timing7, ...] = ("Seed", "Ignite", "Translate", "Bridge", "Weave", "Seal", "Return")

FACES4: tuple[Face4, ...] = ("S", "F", "C", "R")

@dataclass(frozen=True)

class HelmState:

    beat: int                     # 0..419

    phi3: float                   # [0, 2π)

    phi5: float                   # [0, 2π)

    phi7: float                   # [0, 2π)

    vartheta: tuple[float, float, float, float]   # barycentric tilt on S,F,C,R

    handedness: Handedness

    omega_phase: float            # [0, 2π)

    def __post_init__(self):

        if not (0 <= self.beat < 420):

            raise ValueError("beat must be in 0..419")

        if len(self.vartheta) != 4:

            raise ValueError("vartheta must have four coordinates")

        s = sum(self.vartheta)

        if abs(s - 1.0) > 1e-9:

            raise ValueError("vartheta must sum to 1")

def _sector(angle: float, n: int) -> int:

    """

    0-based sector index from a wheel angle.

    """

    twopi = 2.0 * pi

    a = angle % twopi

    return int((a / twopi) * n) % n

def tau3(helm: HelmState) -> Current3:

    return CURRENT3[_sector(helm.phi3, 3)]

def tau5(helm: HelmState) -> Gear5:

    return GEAR5[_sector(helm.phi5, 5)]

def tau7(helm: HelmState) -> Timing7:

    return TIMING7[_sector(helm.phi7, 7)]

def b4(helm: HelmState) -> int:

    """

    4-beat barycentric clock projection on the 420-beat master cycle.

    """

    return 1 + (helm.beat % 4)

def dominant_face(helm: HelmState) -> Face4:

    idx = max(range(4), key=lambda i: helm.vartheta[i])

    return FACES4[idx]

def live_address_tail(helm: HelmState) -> dict:

    """

    Exact live address tail:

      (tau3, tau5, tau7; phi3, phi5, phi7; vartheta; handedness; Omega)

    """

    return {

        "tau3": tau3(helm),

        "tau5": tau5(helm),

        "tau7": tau7(helm),

        "phi3": helm.phi3,

        "phi5": helm.phi5,

        "phi7": helm.phi7,

        "vartheta": helm.vartheta,

        "handedness": helm.handedness,

        "Omega": helm.omega_phase,

        "beat": helm.beat,

        "b4": b4(helm),

    }

def advance_helm(helm: HelmState, dt: int = 1) -> HelmState:

    """

    Advance the live helm by dt beats on the 420-beat master cycle.

    Derived convention:

      every wheel performs one full rotation over 420 beats.

    """

    twopi = 2.0 * pi

    dphi = twopi * (dt / 420.0)

    return HelmState(

        beat=(helm.beat + dt) % 420,

        phi3=(helm.phi3 + dphi) % twopi,

        phi5=(helm.phi5 + dphi) % twopi,

        phi7=(helm.phi7 + dphi) % twopi,

        vartheta=helm.vartheta,

        handedness=helm.handedness,

        omega_phase=(helm.omega_phase + dphi) % twopi,

    )

def tilt_distance(v1: tuple[float, float, float, float], v2: tuple[float, float, float, float]) -> float:

    return sum(abs(a - b) for a, b in zip(v1, v2))

def tilt_to_face(helm: HelmState, face: Face4, strength: float = 0.2) -> HelmState:

    """

    Small lawful tilt correction: changes the metric, not the topology.

    """

    idx = FACES4.index(face)

    v = list(helm.vartheta)

    # pull mass toward preferred face

    delta = strength

    take = delta / 3.0

    for i in range(4):

        if i == idx:

            v[i] += delta

        else:

            v[i] -= take

    # renormalize / clamp

    v = [max(0.0, x) for x in v]

    total = sum(v)

    if total == 0:

        v = [0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25]

    else:

        v = [x / total for x in v]

    return HelmState(

        beat=helm.beat,

        phi3=helm.phi3,

        phi5=helm.phi5,

        phi7=helm.phi7,

        vartheta=(v[0], v[1], v[2], v[3]),

        handedness=helm.handedness,

        omega_phase=helm.omega_phase,

    )

# ------------------------------------------------------------

# Edge-window gating

# ------------------------------------------------------------

def op_family(op: str) -> str:

    if op in {"H+", "H-"}:

        return "shell_ascent"

    if op in {"A+", "A-"}:

        return "archetype_lift"

    if op in {"Tau", "T"}:

        return "chart_transfer"

    if op in {"Q"}:

        return "payload_phase"

    if op in {"O", "H"}:

        return "payload_torsion"

    if op.startswith("+") or op.startswith("-"):

        return "hidden_closure"

    if op.startswith("ZERO["):

        return "zero_tunnel"

    if op.startswith("LOCK["):

        return "live_lock"

    if op == "RefineCloud":

        return "hidden_refine"

    return "generic"

PREFERRED_FACE: dict[str, Optional[Face4]] = {

    "shell_ascent": "S",

    "archetype_lift": "S",

    "chart_transfer": "F",

    "payload_phase": "F",

    "payload_torsion": "C",

    "hidden_closure": "R",

    "hidden_refine": "R",

    "zero_tunnel": None,

    "live_lock": None,

    "generic": None,

}

def edge_window_open(op: str, helm: HelmState) -> bool:

    """

    Hard gate G_e(H(t)) in 0/1 form.

    The specific wheel/face preferences below are an execution convention

    built from the corpus' route-family biases.

    """

    fam = op_family(op)

    cur = tau3(helm)

    gear = tau5(helm)

    timing = tau7(helm)

    face = dominant_face(helm)

    if fam == "zero_tunnel":

        return True

    if fam == "live_lock":

        return True

    if fam == "shell_ascent":

        return (

            cur == "Su" and

            gear == "Lift" and

            timing in {"Ignite", "Bridge"} and

            face == "S"

        )

    if fam == "archetype_lift":

        return (

            cur in {"Su", "Me"} and

            gear == "Lift" and

            timing in {"Ignite", "Weave"} and

            face == "S"

        )

    if fam == "chart_transfer":

        return (

            cur == "Me" and

            gear == "Traverse" and

            timing == "Translate" and

            face == "F"

        )

    if fam == "payload_phase":

        return (

            cur in {"Su", "Me"} and

            gear in {"Lift", "Traverse"} and

            timing in {"Ignite", "Translate"} and

            face == "F"

        )

    if fam == "payload_torsion":

        return (

            cur in {"Me", "Sa"} and

            gear == "Twist" and

            timing in {"Bridge", "Return"} and

            face == "C"

        )

    if fam == "hidden_closure":

        return (

            cur in {"Me", "Sa"} and

            gear in {"Compress", "Traverse"} and

            timing in {"Weave", "Seal", "Return"} and

            face == "R"

        )

    if fam == "hidden_refine":

        return (

            gear == "Compress" and

            timing in {"Seal", "Return"} and

            face == "R"

        )

    return True

def wait_until_open(op: str, helm: HelmState, limit: int = 420) -> tuple[int, HelmState]:

    """

    Wait on the 420-beat clock until G_e opens.

    """

    cur = helm

    for dt in range(0, limit + 1):

        if edge_window_open(op, cur):

            return dt, cur

        cur = advance_helm(cur, 1)

    raise RuntimeError(f"edge never opened within {limit} beats: {op}")

def tilt_first_adjust(op: str, helm: HelmState, max_l1: float = 0.5) -> Optional[tuple[HelmState, float]]:

    """

    Try the tilt-first law:

    if a small legal tilt opens the edge, prefer that before climbing to a higher zero.

    """

    pref = PREFERRED_FACE[op_family(op)]

    if pref is None:

        return None

    if dominant_face(helm) == pref:

        return None

    new_helm = tilt_to_face(helm, pref, strength=0.25)

    d = tilt_distance(helm.vartheta, new_helm.vartheta)

    if d <= max_l1 and edge_window_open(op, new_helm):

        return new_helm, d

    return None

# ------------------------------------------------------------

# Live cost law

# ------------------------------------------------------------

@dataclass(frozen=True)

class LiveWeights:

    alpha: float = 1.0  # shell jumps

    beta: float = 1.0   # phase/chart jumps

    chi: float = 1.0    # archetype lifts

    delta: float = 1.0  # wait time

    epsilon: float = 1.0  # torsion flips

    zeta: float = 1.0   # zoom / zero tunnel

    eta: float = 1.0    # appendix/canopy/hidden closure

    mu: float = 1.0     # tilt correction

def live_cost(word: list[str], wait_time: int, tilt_l1: float, weights: LiveWeights = LiveWeights()) -> float:

    j_shell = sum(op in {"H+", "H-"} for op in word)

    j_phase = sum(op in {"Tau", "T"} for op in word)

    j_archetype = sum(op in {"A+", "A-"} for op in word)

    f_qo = sum(op in {"O", "H"} for op in word)

    z_zoom = sum(op.startswith("ZERO[") for op in word)

    c_appendix = sum(op.startswith("+") or op.startswith("-") or op == "RefineCloud" for op in word)

    return (

        weights.alpha * j_shell +

        weights.beta * j_phase +

        weights.chi * j_archetype +

        weights.delta * wait_time +

        weights.epsilon * f_qo +

        weights.zeta * z_zoom +

        weights.eta * c_appendix +

        weights.mu * tilt_l1

    )

# ------------------------------------------------------------

# Full live compiler

# ------------------------------------------------------------

def canonical_route_live(

    src: MegaLocalNode,

    dst: MegaLocalNode,

    gates: MegaLocalGates,

    helm: HelmState,

    weights: LiveWeights = LiveWeights(),

    prefer_tilt_first: bool = True,

) -> Optional[dict]:

    """

    Full odd/even live compiler.

    Route form:

      HELM · LOCK · ZERO · w_666 · w_chart · w_shell6 · w_15

    """

    base_class = route_class_mega_local(src, dst, gates)

    if base_class == "ILLEGAL":

        return None

    lock = nearest_common_live_lock(src.live_locks, dst.live_locks)

    if lock is None:

        return None

    zero = choose_common_zero(src, dst)

    w_lock = [f"LOCK[{lock}]"]

    w_zero = [f"ZERO[{zero}]"]

    w_outer = outer_word(src.outer, dst.outer)

    w_chart = chart_word(src.chart, dst.chart)

    w_shell = shell6_word(src.payload, dst.payload)

    w_hidden = canonical_hidden_word(src.mask, dst.mask)

    structural_word = w_lock + w_zero + w_outer + w_chart + w_shell + w_hidden

    cur_helm = helm

    scheduled: list[str] = []

    total_wait = 0

    total_tilt = 0.0

    for op in structural_word:

        if edge_window_open(op, cur_helm):

            scheduled.append(op)

            cur_helm = advance_helm(cur_helm, 1)

            continue

        # Tilt-first before waiting

        if prefer_tilt_first:

            adjusted = tilt_first_adjust(op, cur_helm)

            if adjusted is not None:

                new_helm, d_tilt = adjusted

                scheduled.append(f"TILT[{dominant_face(cur_helm)}→{dominant_face(new_helm)}]")

                total_tilt += d_tilt

                cur_helm = new_helm

                # apply op immediately after tilt

                scheduled.append(op)

                cur_helm = advance_helm(cur_helm, 1)

                continue

        dt, opened = wait_until_open(op, cur_helm)

        if dt > 0:

            scheduled.append(f"WAIT[{dt}]")

            total_wait += dt

        cur_helm = opened

        scheduled.append(op)

        cur_helm = advance_helm(cur_helm, 1)

    cls = route_class_mega_local(src, dst, gates)

    # A live route can degrade from EXACT -> RESIDUAL if the path touches unresolved closure.

    # We keep the underlying legality class from the mega-local theorem.

    return {

        "class": cls,

        "lock": lock,

        "zero": zero,

        "initial_helm": live_address_tail(helm),

        "final_helm": live_address_tail(cur_helm),

        "raw_signature": {

            "d_outer": outer_distance(src.outer, dst.outer),

            "d_chart": chart_distance(src.chart, dst.chart),

            "d_shell6": shell6_distance(src.payload, dst.payload),

            "d_hidden15": hidden_distance(src.mask, dst.mask),

        },

        "word_structural": structural_word,

        "word_live": scheduled,

        "wait_time": total_wait,

        "tilt_l1": total_tilt,

        "cost_live": live_cost(scheduled, total_wait, total_tilt, weights),

    }
