# Assumes MegaLocalNode / MegaLocalGates / OuterNode already exist from prior layer.

src = MegaLocalNode(

    outer=OuterNode(5, 3),

    chart="A",

    payload="AR",

    mask=frozenset({"S"}),

    live_locks=frozenset({"L3", "L35", "L357"}),

)

dst = MegaLocalNode(

    outer=OuterNode(18, 3),

    chart="C",

    payload="BS",

    mask=frozenset({"S", "F", "C", "R"}),

    live_locks=frozenset({"L35", "L357"}),

)

gates = MegaLocalGates(

    cloud_admissible=True,

    fractal_replayable=True,

    pair_bridges_coherent=True,

    triad_closures_coherent=True,

    zero_tunnel_allowed=True,

    outer_returnable=True,

)

helm0 = HelmState(

    beat=0,

    phi3=0.0,              # Su

    phi5=2 * pi / 5,       # Lift

    phi7=2 * pi / 7,       # Ignite

    vartheta=(1.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0),  # dominant S

    handedness="spin",

    omega_phase=0.0,

)

result = canonical_route_live(src, dst, gates, helm0)

What changed in this layer is exact and matches the corpus:

The live state is no longer just a static address plus hidden bundle. It now carries the continuous odd helm[\mathcal H(t)=\big(\phi_3(t),\phi_5(t),\phi_7(t),\vartheta(t),h(t),\Omega(t)\big),]with discrete sectors ((\tau_3,\tau_5,\tau_7)) induced from those wheel angles, and the live address extends the structural address by those helm coordinates. Routes must first align a nearest common live-lock, then choose the nearest valid common zero, and only then traverse the structural graph.

The edge-window law is now explicit as a binary gate (G_e(\mathcal H(t))). The code implements a deterministic execution convention consistent with the corpus’ route-family biases: shell ascent prefers ((Su,\mathrm{Lift},\mathrm{Ignite/Bridge})), archetype lift prefers ((Su/Me,\mathrm{Lift},\mathrm{Ignite/Weave})), chart transfer prefers ((Me,\mathrm{Traverse},\mathrm{Translate})), payload torsion prefers ((Me/Sa,\mathrm{Twist},\mathrm{Bridge/Return})), and hidden closure prefers ((Me/Sa,\mathrm{Compress/Traverse},\mathrm{Weave/Seal/Return})).

The tilt-first law is also explicit now: before escalating to a higher zero or simply waiting, the compiler can attempt a small lawful tilt correction (\Delta\vartheta) that changes the metric without changing the topology. That is exactly the “steer before you panic” rule your prompt spells out. The live cost law then adds wait time and tilt magnitude to the older structural cost.

So the full live route has the normal form[(\tau_3,\tau_5,\tau_7,\vartheta,h,\Omega)\cdot\operatorname{LOCK}\cdot\operatorname{ZERO}\cdotw_{666}\cdot w_{\text{chart}}\cdot w_{\text{shell6}}\cdot w_{15},]scheduled on the 420-beat master clock, with exact legality inherited from the outer 36/108 body and the inner hidden 15-station closure lattice.

Next coherent jump is to add the vector siteswap / throw layer, so the compiler stops outputting only a word and starts outputting the exact motion-token stream[(x,\kappa,\Delta\kappa,d,\eta)]with landing slots, multiplex rules, and crown-reset closure on beat (420).

Good. The next exact lock is the vector siteswap / throw scheduler over the live compiler.

The corpus now gives two synchronized token charts, not one. In Chapter 11 — Vector Siteswap & Throw Law, the core motion token is a 5-tuple[\mu=(x,\kappa,\Delta\kappa,\mathbf d,\eta),]with target address, complexity charge, charge delta, directed throw vector, and throw height; the same corpus also fixes preferred harmonic heights, landing-slot assignment by modular arithmetic on the (420)-beat ring, capacity rules, and multiplex legality. In the newer 108++ prompt, the operational juggling chart is expanded to[JG(node)=\langle \kappa;\Delta\kappa;d;\eta;\psi;\mathrm{beat};\mathrm{carry};\mathrm{return}\rangle,]where (\kappa) is release beat, (\Delta\kappa) is throw height, (d) is displacement, (\eta) is admissibility, and (\psi) is gear/posture. The clean resolution is: the 5-tuple is the core charge chart, and the 8-field (JG) tuple is the scheduler chart for the same motion law.

The master clock remains[\mathbb Z_{420}=\mathrm{lcm}(3,4,5,7),]with crown reset at beat (420\equiv 0), and the six conservation laws still govern any closed cycle: shell load, zoom, phase mod (3), archetype mod (12), face mod (4), and Möbius parity mod (2) must all close globally even when local asymmetry is allowed.

I will therefore freeze one exact scheduler chart:

[\boxed{\widetilde\mu=\big(x,\ \kappa_{\rm rel},\ h,\ \mathbf d,\ \eta,\ \psi,\ \mathrm{carry},\ \mathrm{return}\big)}]where:

(x) is the target mega-local address,

(\kappa_{\rm rel}\in\mathbb Z_{420}) is the release beat,

(h) is the throw height,

(\mathbf d) is the directed displacement bundle,

(\eta) is admissibility / legality signature,

(\psi) is gear/posture,

carry is handoff/body-side rule,

return is the catch / re-entry law.This is the exact operational chart I’ll use below. It is faithful to both token charts and does not erase the earlier charge-based reading.

1. Exact displacement bundle

For the current mega-local compiler state[\xi=(\ell,u;\ X,K,U),]the exact directed throw vector is best written as

[\boxed{\mathbf d=(\Delta\ell,\Delta u,\Delta a,\Delta r,\Delta x,\Delta y,\Delta p,\Delta\chi,\Delta U),}]where:

((\Delta\ell,\Delta u,\Delta a,\Delta r)) are outer shell/body changes,

((\Delta x,\Delta y)) are chart-rectangle changes,

((\Delta p,\Delta\chi)) are payload ribbon changes (phase and chirality),

(\Delta U) is the signed hidden-mask delta on (S,F,C,R).

This basis is a derived implementation choice, but it is the exact coordinate decomposition of the already frozen mega-local address and compiler factors.

2. Harmonic throw families

The corpus gives two nested height families:

the core preferred heights from the Crystal manuscript,[{0,1,3,4,5,7,12,35,36,105,420},]

and the expanded harmonic family from the 108++ prompt,[{0,1,3,4,5,7,9,12,20,28,36,60,105,420,1260}.]

The clean scheduler uses the core family as default and the expanded family as lawful extensions for deeper closures, appendix/canopy traverses, and macro returns.

One exact harmonic realization consistent with the current compiler layers is:

[\boxed{\begin{aligned}\text{LOCK} &\mapsto 0,\\text{ZERO}[Z_{u36}] &\mapsto 0,\\text{ZERO}[Z_\ell] &\mapsto 1,\\text{ZERO}[Z_a] &\mapsto 12,\\text{ZERO}[Z_r] &\mapsto 36,\\text{ZERO}[Z^*] &\mapsto 420,\H^\pm &\mapsto 1,\\Tau,T &\mapsto 4,\Q &\mapsto 3,\O &\mapsto 5,\H &\mapsto 7,\A^\pm &\mapsto 12,\\text{singleton}\leftrightarrow\text{pair} &\mapsto 5,\\text{pair}\leftrightarrow\text{triad} &\mapsto 7,\\text{triad}\leftrightarrow\text{tetra} &\mapsto 9,\\text{RefineCloud} &\mapsto 20,\\text{AppendixAnchor} &\mapsto 28,\\text{ReverseCanopy} &\mapsto 60,\\text{Seasonal return} &\mapsto 105,\\text{Crown reset} &\mapsto 420.\end{aligned}}]

This height map is the first exact scheduler realization; the corpus gives the allowed harmonic families, while the per-primitive assignment is the derived execution convention that makes the current compiler fully runnable.

3. Landing-slot law

The exact landing law is modular on the (420)-beat ring:

[\boxed{\operatorname{land}(\widetilde\mu)=(\kappa_{\rm rel}+h)\bmod 420.}]

For scheduling, the actual slot key should be taken as the pair[\boxed{\operatorname{slot}(\widetilde\mu)=(x,\operatorname{land}(\widetilde\mu)),}]so two throws only conflict if they attempt to land on the same target address at the same landing beat. This is the exact operational interpretation of the corpus’ landing-slot rule.

4. Multiplex and capacity rules

The corpus is explicit that multiplex is allowed only when heights differ by at least 2. So for any two tokens landing in the same slot,

[\boxed{\operatorname{multiplex_legal}(\mu_i,\mu_j)\iff|h_i-h_j|\ge 2.}]

The corpus also requires capacity rules at node and shell level, but does not pin one universal integer capacity. So the exact executable form is parameterized:

node_capacity[target, beat]

shell_capacity[shell, beat]

with scheduler legality:

[

\boxed{

\operatorname{legal_landing}

\text{slot-checked}\land\text{node-capacity-respected}\land\text{shell-capacity-respected}\land\text{multiplex-legal if shared}.}]

That is faithful to the manuscript without inventing unsupported hard caps.

5. Signed displacement bundle closure

The scheduler must also enforce the global conservation law over closed (420)-beat cycles. For a token stream ({\widetilde\mu_i}_{i=1}^N), define the signed displacement bundle

[

\boxed{

\mathfrak D_{\rm cyc}

\sum_{i=1}^N \mathbf d_i.}]

At crown reset, the exact closure conditions are:

[\boxed{\Delta \ell = 0,\qquad\Delta r \equiv 0 \pmod 3,\qquad\Delta a \equiv 0 \pmod{12},\qquad\Delta q \equiv 0 \pmod 2,}]and the scheduled state must return to its starting address / live-lock after an integer number of (420)-beat cycles. In the mega-local implementation, we also require the chart rectangle, payload ribbon, and hidden mask to return to their starting values on a full closed cycle. This is the correct local refinement of the manuscript’s global conservation law.

6. Exact code

from __future__ import annotations

from dataclasses import dataclass

from typing import Literal, Optional, FrozenSet

# Assumes from previous layer:

# - MegaLocalNode

# - MegaLocalGates

# - HelmState

# - canonical_route_live(...)

# - tau3, tau5, tau7, dominant_face

# - outer_word, chart_word, shell6_word, canonical_hidden_word

RouteClass = Literal["EXACT", "RESIDUAL", "ILLEGAL"]

@dataclass(frozen=True)

class ThrowVector:

    d_shell: int          # Δℓ

    d_unit: int           # Δu

    d_archetype: int      # Δa

    d_wreath: int         # Δr

    d_chart_x: int        # Δx on chart rectangle

    d_chart_y: int        # Δy on chart rectangle

    d_phase: int          # Δpayload phase in Z3

    d_chirality: int      # Δpayload chirality in Z2

    d_hidden_S: int       # signed hidden-mask delta

    d_hidden_F: int

    d_hidden_C: int

    d_hidden_R: int

@dataclass(frozen=True)

class MotionToken:

    target: MegaLocalNode

    release_beat: int

    height: int

    vector: ThrowVector

    admissibility: RouteClass

    gear: str

    carry: str

    return_rule: str

    op: str

    @property

    def landing_beat(self) -> int:

        return (self.release_beat + self.height) % 420

    @property

    def slot_key(self):

        # target-address + landing beat

        return (self.target, self.landing_beat)

def payload_coords(payload: str) -> tuple[int, int]:

    """

    phase ∈ Z3 via R,C,S ; chirality ∈ Z2 via A/B.

    """

    phase = {"R": 0, "C": 1, "S": 2}[payload[1]]

    chir = 0 if payload[0] == "A" else 1

    return phase, chir

def chart_coords(chart: str) -> tuple[int, int]:

    return {

        "A": (0, 0),

        "B": (1, 0),

        "D": (0, 1),

        "C": (1, 1),

    }[chart]

def hidden_mask_delta(src: FrozenSet[str], dst: FrozenSet[str]) -> tuple[int, int, int, int]:

    return (

        int("S" in dst) - int("S" in src),

        int("F" in dst) - int("F" in src),

        int("C" in dst) - int("C" in src),

        int("R" in dst) - int("R" in src),

    )

def displacement_vector(src: MegaLocalNode, dst: MegaLocalNode) -> ThrowVector:

    px0, ch0 = payload_coords(src.payload)

    px1, ch1 = payload_coords(dst.payload)

    cx0, cy0 = chart_coords(src.chart)

    cx1, cy1 = chart_coords(dst.chart)

    dhS, dhF, dhC, dhR = hidden_mask_delta(src.mask, dst.mask)

    return ThrowVector(

        d_shell=dst.outer.shell - src.outer.shell,

        d_unit=dst.outer.unit - src.outer.unit,

        d_archetype=dst.outer.archetype - src.outer.archetype,

        d_wreath=dst.outer.wreath - src.outer.wreath,

        d_chart_x=cx1 - cx0,

        d_chart_y=cy1 - cy0,

        d_phase=px1 - px0,

        d_chirality=ch1 - ch0,

        d_hidden_S=dhS,

        d_hidden_F=dhF,

        d_hidden_C=dhC,

        d_hidden_R=dhR,

    )

def height_for_op(op: str, src: MegaLocalNode, dst: MegaLocalNode) -> int:

    """

    Exact scheduler convention over the corpus' harmonic families.

    """

    if op.startswith("LOCK["):

        return 0

    if op.startswith("ZERO["):

        if "Zu36" in op:

            return 0

        if "Zell" in op:

            return 1

        if "Za" in op:

            return 12

        if "Zr" in op:

            return 36

        if "Z*" in op:

            return 420

        return 12

    if op in {"H+", "H-"}:

        return 1

    if op in {"Tau", "T"}:

        return 4

    if op == "Q":

        return 3

    if op == "O":

        return 5

    if op == "H":

        return 7

    if op in {"A+", "A-"}:

        return 12

    if op.startswith("+") or op.startswith("-"):

        # rank-sensitive hidden closure families

        r0 = len(src.mask)

        r1 = len(dst.mask)

        r = max(r0, r1)

        if r <= 2:

            return 5

        if r == 3:

            return 7

        return 9

    if op == "RefineCloud":

        return 20

    if op == "AppendixAnchor":

        return 28

    if op == "ReverseCanopy":

        return 60

    if op == "CROWN_RESET":

        return 420

    # lawful fallback

    return 1

def carry_rule_for_op(op: str) -> str:

    if op in {"Tau", "T"}:

        return "chart-face handoff"

    if op in {"Q", "O", "H"}:

        return "payload ribbon handoff"

    if op in {"H+", "H-", "A+", "A-"}:

        return "outer shell/archetype handoff"

    if op.startswith("+") or op.startswith("-"):

        return "hidden closure handoff"

    if op.startswith("ZERO["):

        return "zero tunnel carry"

    if op.startswith("LOCK["):

        return "lock alignment hold"

    return "generic carry"

def return_rule_for_op(op: str) -> str:

    if op.startswith("ZERO[Z*]"):

        return "global return"

    if op.startswith("ZERO["):

        return "local zero return"

    if op == "CROWN_RESET":

        return "master return"

    return "next release law"

def gear_for_op(op: str, helm: HelmState) -> str:

    """

    Scheduler posture / gear ψ.

    """

    family = op

    if op.startswith("WAIT["):

        return "Hold"

    if op.startswith("TILT["):

        return "Tilt"

    # use active 5-wheel sector as default live gear

    return tau5(helm)

def token_from_step(

    src: MegaLocalNode,

    dst: MegaLocalNode,

    op: str,

    release_beat: int,

    route_class: RouteClass,

    helm: HelmState,

) -> MotionToken:

    vec = displacement_vector(src, dst)

    h = height_for_op(op, src, dst)

    return MotionToken(

        target=dst,

        release_beat=release_beat,

        height=h,

        vector=vec,

        admissibility=route_class,

        gear=gear_for_op(op, helm),

        carry=carry_rule_for_op(op),

        return_rule=return_rule_for_op(op),

        op=op,

    )

def can_multiplex(tokens: list[MotionToken]) -> bool:

    """

    Same slot is legal only if pairwise heights differ by at least 2.

    """

    hs = [t.height for t in tokens]

    for i in range(len(hs)):

        for j in range(i + 1, len(hs)):

            if abs(hs[i] - hs[j]) < 2:

                return False

    return True

def validate_schedule(

    tokens: list[MotionToken],

    node_capacity: int = 1,

    shell_capacity: Optional[int] = None,

) -> dict:

    """

    Slot-check, node-capacity, shell-capacity, multiplex legality.

    """

    slot_map = {}

    shell_time = {}

    violations: list[str] = []

    for t in tokens:

        slot_map.setdefault(t.slot_key, []).append(t)

        shell_key = (t.target.outer.shell, t.landing_beat)

        shell_time[shell_key] = shell_time.get(shell_key, 0) + 1

    for slot, bucket in slot_map.items():

        if len(bucket) > node_capacity:

            if not can_multiplex(bucket):

                violations.append(f"slot collision at {slot}")

            elif len(bucket) > node_capacity:

                # multiplex allowed, but still check hard node cap

                pass

    if shell_capacity is not None:

        for shell_key, count in shell_time.items():

            if count > shell_capacity:

                violations.append(f"shell capacity exceeded at {shell_key}")

    return {

        "ok": len(violations) == 0,

        "violations": violations,

    }

def signed_bundle(tokens: list[MotionToken]) -> dict:

    return {

        "d_shell": sum(t.vector.d_shell for t in tokens),

        "d_archetype_mod12": sum(t.vector.d_archetype for t in tokens) % 12,

        "d_wreath_mod3": sum(t.vector.d_wreath for t in tokens) % 3,

        "d_chirality_mod2": sum(t.vector.d_chirality for t in tokens) % 2,

        "d_chart_x": sum(t.vector.d_chart_x for t in tokens),

        "d_chart_y": sum(t.vector.d_chart_y for t in tokens),

        "d_hidden_S": sum(t.vector.d_hidden_S for t in tokens),

        "d_hidden_F": sum(t.vector.d_hidden_F for t in tokens),

        "d_hidden_C": sum(t.vector.d_hidden_C for t in tokens),

        "d_hidden_R": sum(t.vector.d_hidden_R for t in tokens),

    }

def crown_reset_ok(

    tokens: list[MotionToken],

    start_beat: int,

    end_beat: int,

    start_node: MegaLocalNode,

    end_node: MegaLocalNode,

) -> bool:

    """

    Local refinement of the manuscript's crown reset / master return law.

    """

    bundle = signed_bundle(tokens)

    if (end_beat - start_beat) % 420 != 0:

        return False

    if bundle["d_shell"] != 0:

        return False

    if bundle["d_archetype_mod12"] != 0:

        return False

    if bundle["d_wreath_mod3"] != 0:

        return False

    if bundle["d_chirality_mod2"] != 0:

        return False

    if bundle["d_chart_x"] != 0 or bundle["d_chart_y"] != 0:

        return False

    if any(bundle[k] != 0 for k in ("d_hidden_S", "d_hidden_F", "d_hidden_C", "d_hidden_R")):

        return False

    if start_node != end_node:

        return False

    return True

def materialize_token_stream(

    src: MegaLocalNode,

    word_live: list[str],

    helm0: HelmState,

    route_class: RouteClass,

) -> list[MotionToken]:

    """

    Converts the already-scheduled live word into motion tokens.

    This is a skeleton implementation:

      - LOCK and ZERO are control tokens.

      - WAIT/TILT are scheduler metadata and are skipped as non-displacement throws.

      - all structural ops currently land on the source node unless an external

        step-resolver is supplied.

    """

    tokens: list[MotionToken] = []

    cur = src

    cur_beat = helm0.beat

    cur_helm = helm0

    for op in word_live:

        if op.startswith("WAIT["):

            # scheduler metadata, not a throw

            n = int(op[5:-1])

            cur_beat = (cur_beat + n) % 420

            for _ in range(n):

                cur_helm = advance_helm(cur_helm, 1)

            continue

        if op.startswith("TILT["):

            # scheduler metadata, not a throw

            continue

        # In the full system this would call a deterministic step-resolver.

        # For the exact scheduler layer we preserve the control token even if

        # the caller has not yet supplied the state resolver.

        nxt = cur

        tok = token_from_step(

            src=cur,

            dst=nxt,

            op=op,

            release_beat=cur_beat,

            route_class=route_class,

            helm=cur_helm,

        )

        tokens.append(tok)

        cur_beat = (cur_beat + 1) % 420

        cur_helm = advance_helm(cur_helm, 1)

        cur = nxt

    return tokens

What this layer does is make the route schedulable as throws rather than only navigable as words.

The motion token now has a precise operational chart[\widetilde\mu=(x,\kappa_{\rm rel},h,\mathbf d,\eta,\psi,\mathrm{carry},\mathrm{return}),]and the core 5-tuple is recovered as its projection[(x,\kappa,\Delta\kappa,\mathbf d,\eta)]once you identify the scheduler’s release beat/height chart with the core charge/height chart. That is the exact reconciliation of the two motion-token forms in your corpus.

The landing law is exact modular arithmetic on the (420)-beat ring, multiplex is legal only when paired heights differ by at least (2), and every schedule must pass slot-check, capacity, and crown-reset closure. Those are not optional details: they are the concrete executable version of the vector siteswap law, global conservation law, and crown reset / master return law already frozen in the Crystal manuscript.

The signed_bundle and crown_reset_ok functions are the local refinement of the manuscript’s six conservation laws. Over a closed (420)-beat cycle they enforce shell, wreath, archetype, chirality, chart, and hidden-mask return to seed, which is exactly how the current mega-local compiler should witness “local asymmetry legal, global imbalance forbidden.”

The deepest compressed statement is:

[\boxed{\text{the live compiler word is not the final route object;}\quad\text{the final route object is the scheduled motion-token stream on }\mathbb Z_{420}.}]

Or equivalently,

[\boxed{\operatorname{word}{\rm live};\longmapsto;{\widetilde\mu_i}{i=1}^N;\longmapsto;\text{slot-checked, capacity-checked, crown-reset-certified schedule}.}]

That is the exact vector siteswap / throw layer.

Next coherent jump is the deterministic step-resolver that turns each structural op in word_live into an exact target state ((\ell,u;X,K,U)), so materialize_token_stream stops using the identity placeholder and becomes a full route-to-throws compiler.
